He will return home at the end of February (Dentsu News dispatch from the 30th).

Mexican Finance Minister Visits Washington; Related to Silver Issue

Mexico City: Finance Minister Suárez suddenly departed for the United States. On the surface, this trip is for a honeymoon, but in reality, it may not be. Key members of the Ministry of Finance only learned of Mr. Suárez's departure when he was about to leave. It is likely that after arriving in Washington, Mr. Suárez will discuss the general situation of the silver issue with the US Treasury authorities. However, it can be asserted that this trip is not because he feels uneasy about the future of the silver market. As far as Mexico is concerned, as long as silver maintains a market price of about 50 US cents per ounce, the country's silver mining industry can still expect to make a profit. The Mexican government previously deposited 7 million US dollars in a New York bank as collateral for Mexico's debt to the United States. It is generally believed that when Mr. Suárez holds talks with the US government, he will use Mexico's assistance in the US silver policy as an exchange condition for a satisfactory resolution of the country's debt to the United States (Havas dispatch from the 29th).

London: The Financial Times today carried a dispatch from Washington stating that people in Washington believe that the visit of Mexican Finance Minister Suárez to Washington must be related to the US change in its silver purchasing policy. The US change in policy is likely to give priority to purchasing silver from Latin American countries that have concluded or may conclude reciprocal trade agreements. However, this kind of restrictive measure will cause open conflict between the government and the congressional representatives of the silver-producing states. Mr. Suárez will meet with US government officials tomorrow, and will hold a secret meeting with important members of the silver faction on Wednesday (Reuters dispatch from the 30th).

Predictions for 1936; Serious Incident to Occur on Russian-Manchurian Border; Gloom Envelops All of Europe, but War Will Not Occur; War in East Africa Soon to End; Mussolini Uncomfortable in His Position, Increase in Assassinations, World Economy Increasingly Panicked

Paris: French famous seer and prophetess Madame Fraya etc., Today once again made its annual predictions to the Associated Press, saying that Mussolini could not maintain his supreme authority and would be overthrown or defeated next year, Roosevelt would have to win or be re-elected through struggle, or a new figure would ascend the stage, and former President Hoover had no hope. War panic would envelop the whole of Europe throughout the year, but war would not necessarily occur. There will be many disturbances in the Far East, there will be riots in India, and there will be serious incidents on the Russian-Manchurian border. 1936 is the influence of Saturn and Neptune, and Mars is also connected, so there will be many assassinations and deaths. Bank failures, exchange fraud, increased suffering of the people on the mainland in winter, sudden births and ends of love affairs, and increase in mental illness are all things that should happen. As for France, the current government may not last, but Laval himself may not care, because he has been working hard for a long time, and he would be happy to take a rest. France's democratic system will remain unchanged, and Anglo-French relations may be tense from time to time, but the two countries will maintain friendly relations. France, because of its strong defense and strong military power, will not fear any enemy, and will definitely be victorious. Although the clouds of war are spreading, war will not break out. The Italian-Ethiopian war will end soon, because Mussolini wants to get out of it as soon as he gets a little face. Mussolini's power is declining day by day, and Italy's economy will become more and more difficult in the future, and it will be more difficult to be supported by the people. However, Italy has not yet reached the stage of democracy, so even if Mussolini is gone, the successor will still be a dictator, or slightly more lenient. There will be assassinations in Italy, and Mussolini may not escape. There will also be political disturbances and assassinations in Greece, and General Kondylis should be a little wary. There may be a shocking murder case in Austria. The Habsburg dynasty may be restored, but it is difficult to last. The United Kingdom and the United States will be the most prosperous countries, and there will be great progress next year. The United States has gradually become conservative due to its prosperity and recovery. If President Roosevelt does not see this, there will be big problems in the general election. Attempt to Recover Lost Northern Territory: Abyssinian Army Prepares a Large-Scale Counteroffensive; King Will Personally Oversee the Front Lines from Taissy City; Abyssinian Troops Skillfully Avoid Bombardment, Rendering Italian Air Force's Power Ineffective

Rumors circulating in the Abyssinian capital (Akyab) for some time indicate that the Abyssinian army's counteroffensive, aimed at recovering lost territory along the northern front lines, will commence today. Today marks the end of the Abyssinian Christians' fast and the celebration of the Gabriel Feast. King Abyssinia's preparations to travel from Taissy to the northern front are steadily progressing. Abyssinian military headquarters in various locations are extremely active. Unofficial sources suggest that several dozen Italian aircraft are conducting reconnaissance in the Danbian area today. General Nasibu, commander-in-chief of the Abyssinian army in Wogga Aden, is confident about the outcome of the major battle, at least as far as the northern front is concerned. Collins, Reuters' chief correspondent in Abyssinia, spent a week embedded with General Nasibu's forces and met with him in an old two-story house in the village of Gajah, located on a plain, which serves as his headquarters. The army under General Nasibu's command numbers approximately 75,000 men, mostly wearing yellow uniforms, as white ones are easily targeted by aircraft. The soldiers' diet is very simple, consisting of only a quarter of a pound of barley rice soaked in salt water per day, yet they remain remarkably strong. Initially, the Italian army advanced but subsequently retreated. The current front lines appear largely unchanged since the beginning of the war. Both sides claim to occupy the three locations of Gerlogubi, Gorahai, and Walwal. However, based on the situation, it is estimated that an area of approximately eighty miles has become a "no man's land." Walwal, however, seems to still be occupied by Italian sentries. The Italian army's strategy primarily relies on aerial attacks, which initially had a significant psychological impact. At one point, General Nasibu's troops were almost demoralized due to fear. However, after two Italian aircraft were shot down, attacking aircraft dared not fly below three thousand feet from the ground to avoid being hit by rifles, making their bombs inaccurate. Furthermore, the Abyssinian army is now adept at camouflage and has dug bunkers to avoid bombs, thus treating aerial attacks as routine and remaining calm. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

According to a dispatch from our correspondent Oschinat in Akyab, military experts here believe that after occupying the Danbian area of Adigrat, the Abyssinian army will soon advance toward Magal, Axum, and Aduwa. The strategic situation on the front lines has completely changed in the past week. In the preceding two months, the Italian army made successive advances in the Tigray province, advancing rapidly without encountering significant resistance. Now, the Abyssinian army is putting up strong resistance, resulting in heavy casualties on both sides, possibly exceeding those of the previous two months. A major battle may be imminent. The Abyssinian army's plan seems to be to encircle Magal City, where the Italian front lines are most exposed and vulnerable to Abyssinian exploitation. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

According to a dispatch from our correspondent Oschinat in Akyab, fierce fighting is ongoing on the northern front. Italian and Abyssinian forces are frequently engaged in hand-to-hand combat. While the Italian air force wants to inflict heavy damage by dropping bombs, they are hesitant due to the risk of harming their own troops. Instead, they are resorting to machine-gun strafing, hoping to repel the enemy in a more economical and reliable manner. The Abyssinian troops have become accustomed to aerial bombardment. Upon hearing the approaching sound of aircraft, they quickly seek shelter in the forests, leaving the Italian aircraft helpless. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

Imminent Rainy Season Hinders Enemy Advance; Abyssinian Guerrilla Tactics Prove Effective

According to reports from Akyab, Abyssinian guerrilla forces are disrupting the Italian army's lines of communication on the northern front, hindering their continued advance before the rainy season. The so-called "short rainy season" will begin in a few weeks. Aides to the Abyssinian Emperor told the Associated Press today that General Getachew, the Minister of War's main force, may not advance further. Rumors circulating that General Getachew's troops have engaged in fierce fighting with the Italian army are a misinterpretation of the Emperor's telegram on Saturday announcing the Abyssinian victory at Adigrat. General Getachew's troops are currently stationed between Korem and Amba Alagi. Abyssinian guerrilla tactics have proven effective. The Italian army has now abandoned its attack on Amba Alagi. There have been many scattered skirmishes in the past few days, but few major battles. The main forces of the two armies have not yet made contact. (Kuo Min dispatch, 29th)

Italian Army Uses Poison Gas Shells; Abyssinian Government Protests to the League of Nations

According to reports from Akyab, the Abyssinian government today lodged a protest with the League of Nations, accusing Italian aircraft of indiscriminately using gas bombs in the Adigrat battlefield on the northern front, in violation of the Gas Protocol. The number of Abyssinians who have died from these poison gas shells is currently unknown. The Italian use of gas bombs has provoked the Abyssinian tribes.

Aerial Bombardment Kills Innocent Civilians

According to a dispatch from our correspondent Oschinat in Akyab, four Italian aircraft flew to the town of Dagap on the Wogga Aden area of the southern front and bombed it indiscriminately this morning, killing many civilians. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

Libyan Garrison Transferred to East Africa

According to a report from the Daily Telegraph correspondent in Port Said, Egypt, the Italian steamship "Calabria" recently sailed through the Suez Canal from Benghazi, a port in the Italian colony of Libya, carrying a batch of Libyan troops to Massawa, a port in the Italian colony of Eritrea. It seems that Italy has withdrawn a portion of its garrison in Libya, but the reporter did not specify how many troops were withdrawn. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

Italian Cabinet Holds Meeting; Prime Minister Reports on the War Situation in East Africa; Paris Proposals Fail to Satisfy

According to reports from Rome, Mussolini announced at a cabinet meeting today that the Paris peace proposals fall far short of Italy's minimum requirements, especially regarding the security of Italy's borders and the lives of the Italian people. Therefore, Italy has decided to reject them. He then discussed the situation in Eritrea, stating that in order to achieve rapid progress, a major reorganization of transportation is necessary, and a temporary halt to the transport of troops and 100,000 laborers, essential for any colonial war, is absolutely necessary, especially in the mountainous terrain of the Tigray province. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

According to reports from Rome, the Council of Ministers also approved the agreements signed by the government with Austria, Germany, and Switzerland since the imposition of sanctions by various countries. The Italo-Austrian agreement was signed on the 17th of this month, the Italo-German agreement on the 20th of this month, and the Italo-Swiss agreement on the 3rd of this month. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

According to reliable sources in Paris, Prime Minister Laval has received information that Italy is about to initiate peace talks with Britain and France regarding the Abyssinian issue. After the major debate in the Chamber of Deputies last Saturday, Laval narrowly survived with a majority of only twenty votes, and will now proceed with caution, waiting for Mussolini to make the first move before resuming peace negotiations. The Italian army has now halted its advance in Abyssinia and has even been forced to withdraw from several key points to consolidate its positions. (Kuo Min dispatch, 29th)

Vast War Expenses; Italian Finances Suffer Significant Deficit

According to reports from Rome, the final figures for the 1934-1935 fiscal year were released today, showing a deficit of 2,030,000,000 lira. The estimated cost of the war against Abyssinia is 20,000,000 lira per day. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

Laval Overcomes Parliament; French Cabinet's Position Remains Unstable; Political Difficulties Resolved, but Financial Difficulties Persist

According to well-informed sources in London, although the Laval government was able to secure a victory in the Chamber of Deputies on Saturday, it is doubtful that it will be able to survive until January of next year. It is believed that after Laval's victory, Europe will temporarily return to calm, and the tension that has filled the capitals of various countries for the past few weeks may temporarily subside. (Kuo Min dispatch, 29th)

According to reports from London, the foreign exchange market has revealed the financial world's opinion of the French government's double victory in the Chamber of Deputies on Saturday. The closing price of the French franc on Saturday was 74.94, but it has now risen to 74.54. The US dollar has risen from $4.933125 to $4.929375. The discounts on other gold coins against the British pound have also improved. London circles are now asking whether Prime Minister Laval's victory is merely a temporary reprieve, as there may be many other difficulties before the general election. This can be seen from the forward price of the French franc, which has risen by only 32 centimes, with a discount rate of 2.18. It is generally believed that Laval has overcome his most important political difficulties, but many financial difficulties remain, which may yet lead to his downfall, especially the task of raising tens of billions of francs in public debt, which will be difficult without restoring public confidence in the government. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

Both Houses of Parliament Pass the French Budget

According to reports from Paris, the Chamber of Deputies passed the government's full budget for 1936 on the 19th of this month. It was then submitted to the Senate for review, which passed an amendment yesterday with slightly different figures for revenue and expenditure than the original Chamber of Deputies bill. The Chamber of Deputies then re-discussed the matter today and passed the Senate-amended budget bill by a vote of 400 to 170. The 1936 budget bill has therefore been passed. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

Opening of the Fifth French Salon; Exchanging Artwork for Daily Necessities; Bartering is Revived Today

According to reports from Paris, five years ago, a painter named Remy, feeling the impact of the economic crisis on artists and their livelihoods, came up with the idea of establishing a so-called "Trade Salon." The method involves artists publicly displaying their works, allowing visitors to exchange them for food, clothing, or other daily necessities, reviving the ancient practice of bartering. The "Trade Salon" has been very successful since its inception. This year is the fifth edition, and it has recently opened. 210 artists are participating, exchanging landscapes, still lifes, and other works for hams, shoes, and clothing. One particularly stylish painter exchanged a portrait for a car, while another exchanged a nude painting for a live pig. Such examples are too numerous to mention. In addition to exchanging goods, the "Trade Salon" also allows for the exchange of services for artwork. Several painters have exchanged their works for dental treatment from fourteen dentists. Some hotel owners have requested painters to decorate their dining rooms in exchange for free accommodation for a certain period. In fact, this practice is not new. In the past, many famous painters in their early days frequented taverns and were often unable to pay their debts. Some tavern owners, who were fond of art, requested these painters to paint murals for them in exchange for clearing their debts. This is especially common in Paris. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

Guangdong Province Extends Loans to Aid Businesses During the Year-End Period

The Department of Finance drafts loan measures and submits them to the provincial government for provincial bank compliance

Guangzhou Correspondence: Business in Guangdong Province has been increasingly sluggish this year. Bankruptcies before the end of the year are common. The fundamental reason is that the people are poor and their wealth is exhausted. Purchasing power is weak, and most stores see few customers. The City Industry and Commerce Federation and the City Chamber of Commerce recently submitted a report to the Department of Finance, requesting that commercial loans be provided to aid various industries and ensure a peaceful year-end period, so as not to cause a collapse of all businesses. After receiving the report, the Department of Finance considered the decline of business and the difficulties faced by industry and commerce to be true and drafted measures for providing commercial loans for provincial government approval. The Department of Finance's report is as follows: "Guangdong Province has been affected by the global economic downturn in recent years, resulting in market stagnation and economic decline. Various industries and businesses have experienced difficulties in cash flow, and bankruptcies in the banking industry have occurred one after another. One bankruptcy leads to the associated troubles of related businesses or individuals, resulting in unemployment for workers and bankruptcy for rural areas. This is all due to a lack of capital for operation. Last year, to aid businesses, approval was granted for the City Chamber of Commerce to organize a commercial warehouse warrant committee to issue several million yuan in commercial warehouse warrants. However, the results have been minimal. With the Lunar New Year approaching, businesses are accustomed to settling accounts at the end of the year. However, the market is experiencing a financial drought and a bleak outlook. Without a large amount of cash for adjustment, vitality will be exhausted. It is proposed that the Guangdong Provincial Bank provide commercial loans, with the following four measures: The maximum loan amount is 50,000 yuan. The loan is secured by real estate and fixed assets. The loan amount is based on the registered capital, but the maximum amount should not exceed 5,000 yuan. The monthly interest rate is 7%, and the loan term is six months. In addition, the following two points should be clarified. Regarding collateral, in accordance with Article 2 of the Guangzhou City Real Estate Mortgage Temporary Regulations promulgated on July 13, 1934, the mortgage rights will be published. If there is no objection from a third party after thirty days, the contract will take effect. And in accordance with Article 7, after the court receives the mortgagee's application, it will send personnel to assess the base price of the real estate, and after publication, it will be auctioned after thirty days. The original thirty-day deadline will be reduced to fifteen days, as this loan is to aid businesses so that they can safely get through Lunar New Year. Regarding loans, the deadline will be January 23, 1936 (the end of the Lunar Year). With these measures, borrowers will be able to obtain capital to overcome their difficulties, and lenders will be effectively protected from loss. This is a win-win situation. The Provincial Bank agrees with these measures. Therefore, we submit this report to Your Excellency for review. If approved, please instruct the Provincial Bank to comply, for the public good." (24th)

Songjiang: Detective Team Solves Kidnapping Case

Fan Shu's family, a farmer in Mao Kou, Zhou Jia Bang, the fourth district of the county, was robbed by armed bandits on the night of the 29th of last month. Before leaving, they kidnapped a ten-month-old baby boy. The bandits sent a letter to the family, which was intercepted by Yang Shijie, the detective team leader of the Public Security Bureau. On the afternoon of the 29th, when the bandits were scheduled to meet with the victim's family, the police disguised themselves as the victim and went to the appointed location at the Dongta Lane intersection. Two bandits patrolling the road were apprehended by undercover police detectives Shen Guichang and Wei Yunwei. During interrogation, one of them, Mao Jinzhang, admitted to working in the First Branch of the City Forestry Bureau and confessed to kidnapping the child for ransom. He also implicated Zhu Guangyuan, a local resident, as the ringleader. The team leader led detectives to Xitan that night to rescue the hostage but was unsuccessful. They learned that Zhu Guangyuan was hiding at home and arrested him. Zhu claimed to have previously worked for the county as a special agent but denied any involvement in the kidnapping.

Suzhou: Ding Chaowu Visits Suzhou for Inspection

Ding Chaowu, the Provincial Inspector, departed from the province to investigate the administration of officials and the judiciary in various counties. He arrived in Suzhou on the afternoon of the 29th from Changshu and stayed at the Garden Hotel. Zhu Shusheng, President of the High Court, and Lu Yimei, President of the District Court, visited him successively but did not see him. On the morning of the 30th, at 11:00 AM, he inspected the Public Security Bureau. In the afternoon, at approximately 1:00 PM, he went to the County Government, and at 2:00 PM, he was accompanied by County Magistrate Wu Qiyun to inspect the Education Bureau. It is reported that after completing his inspection in Suzhou, Ding will proceed to Kunshan, Taicang, and other counties to examine the administration of officials.

Changshu: Landing Aircraft Damages Crops

The Eurasia No. 16 aircraft, which was forced to land in Mo Cheng, Yin Zhuang, near Changshu, has suffered extensive damage to its internal machinery and cannot take off. Furthermore, recent rain and snow have made the soil muddy and loose, causing the aircraft to sink by a foot. It has not yet been extracted. Mechanics from Shanghai have been dispatched to dismantle the aircraft. However, due to the local temporary workers' lack of experience in this type of work, progress has been slow. A large barge has been hired to transport the disassembled parts to Shanghai. The aircraft has been stranded at the location for five days, attracting thousands of onlookers daily, resulting in the trampling of the wheat crop in the area. The local farmers have engaged lawyer Xu Houyuan to write to the Shanghai company demanding compensation for the losses.

Nantong: County Government Prevents Abuse in Smoking Cessation Efforts

In order to prevent abuse in smoking cessation efforts, the County Government, through a political affairs meeting, approved measures for managing public and private hospitals and private clinics throughout the county, establishing regulations for administering smoking cessation treatment. Any detected abuse will be treated as collusion for fraud.

Hangzhou: Profits and Losses of Banking Industry This Year

Hangzhou banks have begun settling their accounts and interest payments to various clients on the 15th and 20th of this month. Since the implementation of the legal tender system, the China Transportation Bank and other banks have become busier and have been extending their working hours to complete the work. They should be largely finished by tomorrow (31st) and will implement a major settlement starting on New Year's Day, closing for three days. The banking industry has been generally stable this year, with reduced lending due to the economic downturn. There have been no major difficulties. As for profits, the China Bank has the highest, at over 600,000 yuan. The Jiaotong and Ye banks have profits of over 100,000 yuan. Other banks have also made slight profits, but the amounts are limited. Most money shops have not been able to make a profit.

Local News

After Our Country Declared Legal Tender, What's This? Japanese Residents Issue Banknotes

Even if issued in Japan, how can they be used in China? Creating an anomalous example of Japanese people using Japanese currency. National Goods Factory Joint Association requests a serious protest.

The issue of Japanese residents in Shanghai issuing Japanese banknotes and circulating them in the market is being taken seriously by our government and people. The Japanese Embassy has indicated that this move was not implemented by New Year's Day due to insufficient preparation, but it is limited to use between Japanese people. The details are as follows:

Withdrawal of Banknotes Denominated in Chinese Yuan

The Yokohama Specie Bank, the Bank of Korea, and the Bank of Taiwan, all Japanese banks, have been authorized by the Japanese government to issue Japanese banknotes that circulate throughout Japan. At the same time, the Yokohama Specie Bank once issued banknotes denominated in Chinese Yuan in Shanghai, but due to repeated exclusion and the reliable credit of Chinese banks that consecutively issued banknotes, it was unprofitable and the banknotes denominated in Chinese silver coins were all withdrawn. They have not been seen since.

Places Where Japanese Banknotes Are Used

Japanese banknotes denominated in Japanese Yen, which are commonly referred to as "Old Man Tickets" in our country, are commonly used in Dalian, Changchun, Yingkou, and other ports. They can also be used in Shanghai, but only between Japanese people. If Chinese people receive them, they can go to small money shops in the Sichuan Road area and exchange them for Chinese banknotes according to the telegraphic transfer rate announced daily by the Central Bank. However, a discount is required as a commission for the small money shop.

Japanese Businesses Request to Increase Banknote Issuance

Japanese residents in Shanghai, in view of the overall economic downturn, intend to increase capital by requesting Japanese banks to increase the issuance of Japanese banknotes for use in Shanghai. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency inquired yesterday with Izumimizu, a member of the Information Department of the Japanese Embassy. According to him, the issue of issuing Japanese banknotes is "not issued in Shanghai, but still issued in Japan, and carried to Shanghai for use." "Due to insufficient preparation, it is not possible to implement on New Year's Day." "If issued, it will be limited to use between Japanese people" and "cannot be extended to the entire market."

Our Country Attaches Importance to Japanese Banknote Issuance

Our government and banks are paying close attention to the issue of issuing Japanese banknotes. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency interviewed Secretary-General Lin of the Bank Association yesterday. According to him, Japanese residents in China have been using Japanese banknotes among themselves for a long time. If they want to promote its use between Japanese people and Chinese people, it would have a great impact on our country's entire currency system. It is questionable whether our people can accept it.

National Goods Factory Joint Association Requests to Prohibit It

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Joint Association sent telegrams yesterday to Finance Minister Kong and Industry Minister Wu, stating: "The Xinwenbao reported on the 30th of this month that Japanese residents in Shanghai are issuing Japanese banknotes, scheduled to be used starting on New Year's Day of next year. If true, it would disrupt our country's economic unification, undermine the policy of using legal tender, and have a significant impact on the future of industry and commerce. We respectfully request that you investigate and issue a serious protest, and issue an order prohibiting its use, in order to maintain sovereignty and value the currency system."

Eurasia's Third Giant Aircraft Arrives at Aircraft Factory Yesterday for Inspection

Scheduled to join the Shanghai-Xinjiang Airline after New Year's Day. Li Jingcong held a banquet yesterday afternoon for the four pilots.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation's third giant aircraft began its machinery inspection and painting procedures yesterday. It can be completed in the coming days, and it will join the Shaanxi-Lanzhou section of the Shanghai-Xinjiang route after New Year's Day. General Manager Li Jingcong hosted the four pilots at a banquet yesterday afternoon.

Third Giant Aircraft Inspection and Painting

The Junkers-52 giant aircraft leased by the company from the German Lufthansa arrived at Longhua Airport at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, piloted by four German pilots, including the famous German pilot Klaus. General Manager Li Jingcong led staff and guests from all walks of life in a warm welcome ceremony. Yesterday, according to company secretary Zha Zhenhu, the company instructed its mechanical personnel to send workers to the machinery factory at Longhua Airport this morning (yesterday morning) to begin inspecting all the aircraft's parts and simultaneously paint and repaint the national emblem and company logo. It is expected to be completed entirely in the coming days. The company decided to first deploy the aircraft to the Shaanxi-Lanzhou section of the Shanghai-Xinjiang route, and then transfer it to other routes for use. The official date of participation is expected to be after New Year's Day.

Yesterday Afternoon Hosting the Four German Pilots

Eurasia Aviation Corporation's General Manager Li Jingcong, in order to show the hospitality to the four German pilots, who travelled all the way from Germany, hosted a wash-the-dust banquet for them at the Xinghualou Restaurant on Fourth Racecourse Road at 12:00 noon yesterday. The four pilots, including pilot Klaus, co-pilot Duss, communications officer Bauliequan, and mechanic Laukeshan, attended the banquet. They were accompanied by German Association President Waldehmen, Lufthansa's Shanghai representative Walde, and other German residents. Li Jingcong delivered a welcome speech, followed by a reply from Klaus. The guests departed happily at 1:00 PM. Lau will remain in China for three or four weeks to visit scenic spots in Suzhou and Hangzhou, and is scheduled to return home at the end of next month. The other three pilots are scheduled to return home by ship next week.

Zhu Qin'ao Transferred to Xi'an

Zhu Qin'ao, the Shanghai Station Manager and Secretary of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, has handled all of the station's reforms and matters appropriately since being appointed by Manager Li. The station's business is thriving, and Li is grateful for having him. However, with the opening of the Shaanxi-Chengdu route, the affairs have become more complicated than those of the Shanghai Station. In order to select talented people, Zhu has been transferred to the Xi'an Station as Manager. Liang Yun, the Xi'an Station Manager, will replace him at the Shanghai Station.

Datong Runs Aground in Yangxi

Forward Cabins Take on Water, Rupturing Four Holes. Must Be Extensively Repaired Before Proceeding to Hankou

The Datong steamer, owned by Dada Company and rented from Ping An Company, left Shashi bound for Hankou. On the morning of the 28th of this month, it reached Yangxi when heavy fog caused it to run aground. The bottom of the ship became mired in a pebble beach, and its heavy weight caused four holes to rupture in the forward cabins, causing significant damage and creating a dangerous situation. Fortunately, the Xiafei steamship came by and the Datong shipowner asked for assistance. The Xiafei towed the Datong ship to a point where, by 10:00 AM of the 28th, with the tide rising, it was able to pull it free. With its engine intact, the Datong was able to proceed to Shashi, where the captain was able to temporarily repair the four holes in the forward cabins with cement and planks. The Datong then sailed from Shashi on the 29th towards Hankou, where it is expected to arrive today. It is reported that, although rescued, the damage sustained by the ship when it ran aground was significant and will require extensive dry dock repairs.

Wang Jingwei Receives Artificial Blood Transfusion Again Yesterday

Mr. Wang Jingwei's spirits have been somewhat down in the last few days. Yesterday morning, Dr. Noel injected him with another 500 cubic centimeters (500 C.C.) of artificial blood and strongly advised him not to receive any guests.

I pray for your attention. Respectfully addressed to Madam Ouyang Lizheng, wife of Tang, Wu Tiecheng." Today is the Annual Bank Closing; Receipts and Disbursements are More Numerous; All Industries are Steadily Passing Through

The Money Trade Association Will Hold a General Meeting Today to Approve the Final Closing Date; The Municipal Government, Upon Order, Promulgates the Purpose of Currency Reform

Today is December 31st, the last day of the bank's annual closing. The receipts and disbursements of both the banking and money industries are numerous. The Money Trade Association will hold a regular meeting of its members today to approve the date of the annual final closing. All industries are steadily passing through without other concerns. The Municipal Government, upon order, promulgates to the people to understand the purpose of currency reform. The details are recorded below:

Banks Conduct Annual Closing

After the savings and commercial departments of each bank began paying interest on December 15th and 20th, respectively, all overdrafts were fully cleared today. Yesterday, the banks handled closing matters, and the internal office hours were extended to 12:00 PM. Today is the last day of the annual closing, and internal office hours will be further extended. The banks will be closed for three days for the New Year starting tomorrow. It is expected that the banks will be able to make a profit due to cautious lending during this overall economic downturn. As for the profit report, it will be released after today.

Receipts and Disbursements of Both Industries are More Numerous Yesterday

Yesterday was the second to last day of the bank's annual closing, and the receipts and disbursements of both the banking and money industries were more numerous. The total amount of new bills exchanged at the bank clearing house has increased to 33,345,679.16 national currency, of which 5,443,414.47 was collected on behalf of the money industry. The interest rate for public bill clearing is one jiao per thousand yuan per day, and the discount rate for public bills is one jiao five fen per thousand yuan per day. The market interest rate for foreign currency clearing in the money industry is also one jiao per thousand yuan per day.

All Industrial and Commercial Enterprises Steadily Pass the End of the Year

A reporter from the New Sound News Agency learned from industrial and commercial enterprises yesterday that all industrial and commercial enterprises can steadily pass the bank closing in the 24th year. Although today is the last day, no unfortunate events are expected to occur. As for the final closing date for all industries in the 24th year, it will arrive in an instant. All industries are now preparing for it. Although it is more serious than the bank's annual closing, since the government's new currency system was implemented, the market's chips have increased. At the same time, after the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications handled interbank lending and overdrafts, and the three banks adjusted the money industry, they also made special accommodations for all industries, so all industries can steadily pass.

The Money Trade Association Holds a Regular Meeting Today

The Money Trade Association decided that January 23rd will be the final closing date for the 24th year of the Republic of China, and decided to hold a regular meeting of its members at 1:00 PM today at its association on Ningbo Road. In addition to approving the final closing date, it will also determine the interest rate for December and prepare all preparations before the final closing. Because today is the last day of the bank's annual closing, the receipts and disbursements will inevitably be very busy. The office hours of each money shop will therefore be extended. Starting tomorrow, the New Year holidays will be two days, according to industry regulations.

The Municipal Government, Upon Order, Promulgates to the People

After the Ministry of Finance announced on November 4th that the banknotes of the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications are legal tender, all sectors have complied with it, and it has been quite effective. Various industries have gradually become active, and all believe that the government's move is very appropriate. The Shanghai Municipal Government, upon order from the Executive Yuan, relayed an order to earnestly promulgate to the people to understand the purpose of this decision to reform the currency system in order to facilitate its progress, and has also ordered its subordinates to comply with it.

Exerting Efforts to Cooperate in the Arrest of Opium Smokers and Eliminate the Opium Atmosphere; Registration of Opium Smokers in This City Will Be Completed Today; Hereafter, Opium Offenders Must Be Sent to the Headquarters for Legal Action; Today is the Last Day of Publicity, Hoping that Opium Smokers Will Awaken

The registration of opium smokers in this city has been ongoing for six months, from July 1st to today (31st). Today marks the completion of the registration work for opium smokers in this city. After 6:00 PM, registration will be closed. From tomorrow onwards, opium offenders who are arrested will be sent to the Garrison Headquarters, where they will be sentenced to imprisonment for six months to two years, and fined up to 300 yuan. Those with opium addiction will be given a deadline to receive medical treatment and ordered to quit. To cooperate in the arrest of opium smokers in the concessions, the Public Security Bureau also received a reply from the police department of the Public Concession, agreeing to order its subordinates to handle the matter. Therefore, there is no problem in eliminating the opium atmosphere in this city. As for the anti-opium authorities in this city, they will also mobilize today to conduct a final publicity campaign in the jurisdiction of this city, hoping that opium smokers will finally awaken. The details are recorded below:

Opium Smoker Registration Ends Today

The registration of opium smokers in this city has now reached the final mandatory period. Today is the last day to complete the registration of opium smokers in this city, in accordance with the telegram from President Chiang. For self-surrendering opium smokers, the last remaining opportunity is fleeting. In order to do its best to persuade opium smokers to awaken, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, in addition to sending investigators to cooperate with police officers to vigorously investigate and arrest opium smokers in areas with the most opium smokers, such as the old North Gate and West Gate, also sent Dai Lizhen, the section chief of the opium smoker section, to cooperate with all members of the Municipal Anti-Opium Committee to personally conduct publicity in the city, persuading opium smokers to surrender. Yesterday was the day before the deadline for opium smoker registration, so opium smokers who surrendered were very enthusiastic, totaling 450 people. Nearly 300 opium offenders were also arrested. Today, Section Chief Dai and others will continue to conduct publicity. After office hours in the afternoon, registration will be closed. From tomorrow onwards, opium smokers who are arrested without a license, regardless of whether they are old or sick, will not be issued a certificate of opium cessation, and will be sent to the Garrison Headquarters in this city to be sentenced in accordance with Article 8 of the Provisional Regulations for Punishing Opium Crimes, to imprisonment for six months to two years, and fined up to 300 yuan. Those with opium addiction will be given a deadline to receive medical treatment and ordered to quit. In addition, the Public Security Bureau previously stated that cunning opium smokers in the urban area who are being strictly investigated will inevitably flee to the concessions, and the concession authorities are also very serious about anti-opium efforts, so it specifically requested to find a way to cooperate in the arrest. If any citizens report or various agencies request cooperation in the arrest, they will be notified at any time and personnel will be dispatched to cooperate in the arrest. It is learned that the police department of the Public Concession Bureau has replied to the bureau, ordering its subordinates to handle the matter. Therefore, there is no problem in cooperating in the arrest of opium smokers in the special zone.

Measures for Hospitals Designated to Undertake Opium Cessation

In addition to the Shanghai South and Shanghai North Opium Cessation Hospitals for criminals and the soon-to-be-established temporary opium cessation hospital, which are free of charge, the city authorities have specially formulated measures for hospitals that charge fees and undertake temporary opium cessation work, with strict regulations on fees, so as to avoid the abuse of charging excessive fees and placing an excessive burden on opium cessation patients. These measures will be implemented after being reviewed by the municipal government. The full text of the measures is recorded below: Measures for the Management of Hospitals Designated to Undertake Temporary Opium Cessation Work in This City. In order to promote opium cessation work and facilitate opium smokers to pay for opium cessation, the city may select suitable hospitals from the hospitals registered and approved by the Municipal Health Bureau to undertake temporary opium cessation work. Hospitals designated to undertake temporary opium cessation work shall comply with the provisions of these measures in handling the admission and discharge of opium cessation patients and all procedures. Each designated hospital shall record in detail the name, age, gender, origin, occupation, address, addiction type, and treatment records of opium cessation patients, and keep them properly for inspection. Each designated hospital may require opium cessation patients to prepay fees or find a guarantor. Each hospital may charge opium cessation patients according to the following regulations: A. First-class ward: 4 to 6 yuan per person per day, including food and medical expenses. B. Second-class ward: 2 to 3 yuan per person per day, including food and medical expenses. C. Third-class ward: 1 yuan per person per day, including food and medical expenses. D. All injections, medicines, and tonics may be charged separately by each hospital after consultation with the opium cessation patient. Opium cessation patients must be hospitalized for treatment and may not leave the hospital freely. They may only be issued a certificate of opium cessation by the treatment hospital if the treatment hospital believes that they have completely quit opium. The format of this certificate will be determined separately. Each hospital, after an opium cessation patient has completely quit opium, shall immediately fill out a triplicate report form, send two copies to the Public Security Bureau and the Health Bureau for reference, and keep the remaining copy for future reference. (The format of this report form will be determined separately.) They shall also fill out a monthly opium cessation performance report in quadruplicate at the end of each month and submit it to the Health Bureau for review. Any opium cessation certificate issued by a hospital that has not been approved to undertake temporary opium cessation work will be considered invalid by the municipal opium cessation authorities. The Municipal Public Security Bureau and Health Bureau may send personnel to the designated hospitals at any time to inspect and supervise opium cessation work, and may also randomly select people who have quit opium from each hospital and send them to the municipal opium cessation agency for verification. If a designated hospital violates the provisions of these measures or has other malpractices, its designated qualification may be revoked at any time upon discovery. These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau Announces Collection of Land Value Tax for the 25th Year; Limited to Two Months from January 16th; Tax Payment Certificates Will Now Be Issued

The Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau issued Bulletin No. 319 yesterday, stating, "It has been investigated that the first installment of the provisional land value tax for the 25th year, which should be collected in Districts 1 to 7 of the South Shanghai District, Districts 1, 2, 4, 5, and 6 of the Zhabei District, Districts 5, 6, and 8 of the Yinxiang District, Districts 2, 3, 5, and 6 of the Yangjing District, Districts 1 to 4 of the Fahua District, and District 1 of the Pusong District, will be levied starting on January 16th of the 25th year, and must be paid within two months from the date of levy, until March 15th of the 25th year. Those whose land is in the South Shanghai District should bring the receipt from the previous period and pay at the South Shanghai Tax Collection Office of this Bureau at Maojia Lane, Outer Malu, Nanshi. Those in the Zhabei and Yinxiang Districts should bring the receipt from the previous period and pay at the North Shanghai Tax Collection Office of this Bureau at Datong Road, Zhabei. Those in the Yangjing District should bring the receipt from the previous period and pay at the East Shanghai Tax Collection Office of this Bureau at Chunjiang Wharf, Pudong. Those in the Fahua and Pusong Districts should bring the receipt from the previous period and pay at the West Shanghai Tax Collection Office of this Bureau at the intersection of Roberts Road and Binlang Road. If the payment is overdue, it will be pursued in accordance with Article 8 of the Provisional Land Value Tax Collection Regulations and Article 24 of the Implementation Rules, and interest will be charged on the amount owed, as well as collecting the income from the land and auctioning it to offset the price according to the number of years in arrears, in order to comply with the regulations and emphasize tax revenue. It has also been investigated that when taxpayers pay the land value tax, they must bring the receipt from the previous period for inspection. Now, because this receipt has matters such as land transfer, collection and use, merger and measurement, or registration, it must be submitted to the Land Bureau as evidence of tax payment and management, so that when continuing to pay taxes, it is necessary to report to this Bureau, verify the facts, and issue a certificate of tax payment before it can be paid. If the procedures are not clear, the payment time will inevitably be delayed. In order to facilitate taxpayers, this Bureau has formulated remedial measures, planning to issue a tax payment certificate to each taxpayer when they pay the first installment of the 25th year and make up for the land value tax from the previous period, indicating the year, tax period, and precautions to be taken when paying taxes. In the future, holding this certificate to pay taxes will eliminate the need to present the receipt from the previous period, in order to be simple and convenient. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government for record and mailing this period's notification, this announcement is jointly issued, and all taxpayers should abide by it and pay within the time limit, without delay, lest they be punished. If the notification has not yet been received, they should, within the time limit, provide the land location, diagram number, and present address or mailing address to the Bureau for verification and resending of the duplicate, and still pay at the office with the receipt from the previous period and receive the tax payment certificate for application, without error. This bulletin, Cai Zengji, Director."

The French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association Held its Fourth Representative Congress Yesterday; Du Yuesheng, Huang Jinrong, and Others Were Elected as Executive and Supervisory Committee Members; Lu Bohong, Zhang Xiaolin, and Others Were Elected as Chinese Directors

The Fourth Representative Congress of the Shanghai French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association was held yesterday at 2:00 PM in the Central Bank Building. Du Yuesheng and 14 others were elected as executive committee members, Huang Jinrong and 4 others were elected as supervisory committee members, and Lu Bohong and 4 others were elected as Chinese directors and committee members. Cheng Zhisun's vacancy was filled by Zhang Fayao in a re-election. A reporter from the New New News Agency separately recorded the details as follows:

Attending Representatives

In addition to Mao Yun of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Geng Jiaji of the Municipal Government, and Zhao Tiezhang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, the attendees yesterday included Li Weiliang, Zhang Shishi, He Yuanming, Zheng Zenan, Du Gang, Gu Wensheng, Wang Deyan, Dong Kechang, Ge Weian, Ge Zitan, Lu Tingjian, Tang Jingxi, Gong Jingyan, Cai Hongtian, Chen Dezhang, Zhu Wende, Dai Chunfeng, Zhang Xiangtang, Wang Shunfa, Shang Mujang, Qu Zhenhua, Jin Liren, Qian Jia gui, Huang Xianggu, Mao Derun, Bei Zairong, Wu Guowei, Zhang Gengshan, Liu Fuxiang, Wu Xiu, Huang Baoxiang, Zhu Lanmao, Sheng Zhiren, Zhou Qinfu, Ye Ruizhai, and 43 others. Qi Yunqing, Xue Fuji (representing Chen Baohua), and Dong Lizhang were present as observers.

Congress Order

Everyone stood at attention, paid the highest respect to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Premier, and bowed three times. The chairman respectfully read the Premier's will, observed a moment of silence, the chairman made a report, delivered a speech, gave a work report, discussed proposals, handled temporary motions, held elections, reported the election results, took photos, and adjourned the meeting.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremonial salutations, Du Yuesheng, Huang Xianggu, Zhu Wenqi, Gong Jingyan, and Shang Mujang were nominated as the presidium, and Zhang Shishi was the secretary. The chairman's report on the work of the past year briefly stated that the association's position is to seek benefits for the Chinese taxpayers in the concession. All matters, whether passive or active, that are related to the residents of the concession are diligently undertaken. The French authorities are also able to respect public opinion, and all legitimate protests are accepted. Therefore, the citizens of the concession directly and indirectly benefit from it. The association is self-satisfied with what it has done in the past two years. The following is an excerpt of the more important cases: The Shanghai Municipal History Museum sought historical materials from the French Concession; searched for and compiled the Sino-French New Agreement signed by the French for the expansion of the concession; repeatedly requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance to subsidize the association's operating expenses; achieved complete victory in the Chen Juchang carpentry protest against the health donation; residents of Malong Road, Father Jin Road, Qianjiatang, and Avenue Joffre requested the Municipal Council to exempt them from increased house donations; the Fenjiu Industry Association requested exemption from increased alcohol donations; the French Concession provided subsidies for primary and secondary schools; negotiations to increase the number of Chinese directors; taxpayers requested exemption from house donations for public welfare projects; and Caishi Road and Bai'er Road requested the construction of sidewalks.

Discussion of Proposals

After the chairman's report, the representatives of the Party and government organs delivered speeches, and then the discussion of the following proposals began: Wu Kaisheng proposed that the association should request the French authorities to increase the number of Chinese directors in proportion to the Chinese population. Shanghai Municipal Council Reviews the Rent Law; The Municipal Federation Requests Setting Rent Standards For a Reason; The Disguised Double Rent Should Be Strictly Prohibited

In recent years, the rent problem in Beijing and Shanghai has been entangled. The Executive Yuan has convened representatives from the Ministry of Finance and other departments and representatives from Beijing and Shanghai to review the draft of the Rent Dispute Mediation Law. In order to make it suitable for the actual situation in Shanghai, the Shanghai Municipal Government transferred it to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Council for their opinions. In addition to the Municipal Party Headquarters responding, the Municipal Council also convened a review meeting on the 18th of this month. Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Chen Guangfu, Du Yuesheng, and Xu Yongzuo were present. Regarding Article 2 of the draft law, "House rent shall be determined by the local competent authorities in consideration of local circumstances and submitted to the higher authorities for approval. The maximum limit of the aforementioned rent standard shall not exceed 12% of the annual interest rate of the total land price and construction cost." Although the interest rate in this article is based on the Land Law and local facts, such as the interest rate in Shanghai, which is generally below 1%, and the profit of the rent, which is generally only 5% to 6% of the land price and construction cost, the Shanghai Municipal Federation requests the authorities to set the rent standard at 5%, which is justified. According to economic principles, the more developed the society, the lower the interest rate. The spirit of legislation is to hope for the progress of society, and it seems that this standard should not be too high. It should be limited to 10% at most, so that the high interest rate in the inland can gradually be equalized. This is not only suitable for the situation in Shanghai, but also in line with the spirit of legislation. Article 3 of the original draft states, "The house rent mentioned in the preceding article refers to the amount paid periodically by the tenant to the landlord for the use of the house. Other matters relating to house rent in accordance with local customs may be determined by the local competent authorities in consideration of local circumstances, within the scope of not conflicting with the law." It is explained that "In addition to restricting the excessively high security deposits in various places, there are other similar facts about house rent in various places, which may be approved within the scope of not conflicting with the law." Since the rent has a standard, this disguised double rent should be strictly prohibited. Therefore, the second half of Article 3 can be deleted. For the sake of taking into account customs and protecting the legitimate interests of landlords, it can only be stipulated that the security deposit can be collected up to two months' rent, so as to avoid landlords using Article 3 to charge various fees. Article 4 seems to be determined for both sides, and the rent standard is revised every five years. In fact, the collection of rent is calculated according to the interest rate of the land price and construction cost. After the house is built, its construction cost does not increase or decrease with the price level thereafter, and it often decreases due to annual depreciation. The only changes are the land price and the market interest rate. However, the increase in land price is caused by the public, not the landlord, and the landlord should not enjoy its benefits alone. Now that it is not attributed to the public, the result of the increase in land price is that the property has already increased, and then the rent is increased for the tenant. The double benefit is too great. As for the change in interest rate, real estate is a more secure investment, and the profit should not be in the same proportion as the general interest rate. If it is for the sake of general people's livelihood, it is feasible to reduce the rent when the interest rate is low (such as when the house is old), and it is difficult to increase the rent when the interest rate is high. Therefore, if the rent standard is revised every five years, it is feared that there will be many disputes at that time. Moreover, there are many provisions in the lease part of the Civil Law on Obligations. The law seems that it is not necessary to stipulate it in another article." It is heard that the Municipal Council has replied to the Municipal Government accordingly.

New Life Movement Commemorative Stamps: Four Colors – Red, Blue, Light Green, and Deep Green – Inscribed with the Words "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame"; Post Office to Issue on New Year's Day

The Shanghai Postal Administration has decided to begin issuing New Life Movement commemorative stamps from New Year's Day next year. According to a Datong News Agency reporter's inquiry with the Post Office, the facts are as follows:

Four Different Colors

These commemorative stamps are approximately one and a half times larger than regular stamps, rectangular in shape, and vary in color according to their denomination. The one-yuan stamp is light red, the two-jiao stamp is blue, the five-fen stamp is light green, and the two-fen stamp is deep green, totaling four colors, i.e., a complete set is valued at one yuan, two jiao, and five fen.

New Life Movement Commemorative Stamps

Design and Wording

The artwork for these stamps was recently created by the Peiping Printing Bureau and is completely different from regular stamps. The stamps are all engraved with the words "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame," as well as "New Life Movement Commemorative." However, the font and the position of the inscription vary according to the denomination of the stamp. The New Life Movement logo is engraved in the center of each stamp.

Issuance on New Year's Day

According to inquiries made by the Datong News Agency reporter at the Postal Administration, the Shanghai postal district has received over 100,000 yuan worth of these stamps from the General Post Office. The Post Office will be closed on New Year's Day as per usual, so actual sales will begin on January 2nd. The sales period is set for six months, but the stamps can still be used as usual within three months after the sales period ends.

Xu Shiying's Intention to Resign Has Been Abandoned: The Executive Yuan Agreed to Allocate Additional Funds; Xu Scheduled to Go to the Capital on the Evening of the 2nd

Mr. Xu Jingren, Chairman of the Central Relief Committee, had repeatedly requested the Executive Yuan to resign from all his positions due to the committee's financial difficulties. Premier Chiang believed that Mr. Xu had been in politics for ten years, had always been honest and self-disciplined, and had personally visited various places despite the frequent disasters over the years. His spirit of service was admirable, and he was urged to continue his work to benefit the disaster victims. Later, Mr. Xu insisted that the committee's operating expenses were too low, averaging a deficit of three to four hundred yuan per month. Not only did all the staff members feel hungry while working, but there were also many obstacles to the work, making it like a skilled housewife struggling to cook without rice. Therefore, he submitted three more resignations. Premier Chiang, puzzled by Mr. Xu's insistence on resigning, specially summoned Mr. Zhu Qinglan, a standing committee member of the committee, to the capital to inquire in detail. After Mr. Zhu explained the above difficulties, Premier Chiang said that a shortage of three hundred yuan per month was not a problem. He sent a telegram to Mr. Xu, still urging him to stay, and instructed the Ministry of Finance to allocate additional funds to the committee on a monthly basis. If Mr. Xu must resign, Mr. Zhu should take over the position, and the national government would offer Mr. Xu a new position so that he would not retire. Mr. Zhu telegraphed Premier Chiang's intentions to Mr. Xu, stating the government's earnest reliance on him. Therefore, Mr. Xu's intention to resign has been completely abandoned. He goes to the Relief Committee as usual every day to handle important matters and is scheduled to go to the capital on the evening of January 2nd to seek instructions on winter relief matters.

Citywide Pawnshop Industry: To Shorten Pawn Period Tomorrow; Uniformly Changed to Twelve Months; Pawn Interest Still Handled According to Old System

The Shanghai Pawnshop Industry Association, in accordance with the request of its members to maintain their livelihoods, has received approval from the Municipal Government to shorten the standard pawn period to twelve months. This was resolved at a joint meeting of old and new pawnshop owners on the 17th of this month and will be officially implemented on January 1st, 1936 (tomorrow). According to a reporter from the Industrial News Agency's interview with Mr. Lian Jieren of the industry, he said that the decision to shorten the pawn period was a last resort, and the original state would be restored as soon as the city's economy recovered. The industry is almost completely unified on shortening the pawn period, with 45 old pawnshops and 27 new pawnshops. The pawn interest will still be 1.8%, plus 0.2% for warehouse rent. It is feared that the original pawn period would be shortened further due to the short original duration.

Gu Peiyuan: Confesses to Defrauding a Large Sum of Money; Conscience Compelled Him to Confess the Truth; Another Person Named Ye Also Accuses Him of Being Deceived

Zhu Shien (also known as Junmu, Zhanfu), a real estate merchant from Yin County, Zhejiang Province, residing at No. 25 Anren Street, Xinbeimen, Nanshi, owns a lot of money. His eldest son, Zhu Yinting, is 17 years old and studies at Yinghua Shuguan. Recently, he was defrauded of a huge sum of 45,115 yuan in foreign currency by Gu Peiyuan (also known as Naiping), the owner of the Yuanji Driving School at No. 44 Guangdong Road, through methods such as physiognomy and divination, causing him to speculate in gold speculation. After reporting the case, the General Patrol Room arrested Gu and confiscated about 30,000 yuan, which was sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. This has been reported in detail in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Qian Hongye, the criminal division chief of the First Special Court, continued the interrogation in the first criminal court. Gu Peiyuan hired lawyers Du Jimei and Xi Shichang to defend him. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated that the defendant had completely denied the facts of the case last time, but during the adjournment period, the defendant had fully confessed to everything in the police station and had written a confession. It was also found that the defendant had published advertisements in the newspaper under the name Fang Juelu, offering free physiognomy, and the location was in the Yuanji shop. He then presented the confession newspapers to the court. Subsequently, Niu Sheng, the principal of Yinghua Shuguan, filed a case, proving that Zhu Yinting's age was sixteen years old according to British calculation, but his grades in all subjects were poor, so he was in the lowest grade. Dai Weiyang, a trainee at the Yuanji shop, also filed a case, proving that Zhu Yinting came to Yuanji to learn to drive, and Gu helped him with his fortune-telling, saying that he had mourning clothes. Later, Zhu's mother died, and Zhu firmly believed in Gu's words. Later, Gu asked me to investigate Zhu's situation and the number of people in his family, and I conducted the investigation for him. When questioned, Gu Peiyuan confessed that he did not recognize it last time because the plaintiff had no evidence. Later, he was driven by his conscience, so he fully recognized it, and then he explained the details of the matter in detail. As for the method of displaying words on red paper, he used Ming Panhua water to write on the paper, covered it with incense ash, and the words would appear. Police lawyer Wang stated that a person named Ye had come to report that he had also been deceived by the defendant, so further investigation was needed. Qian, the chief judge, approved it and scheduled another interrogation.

Such behavior was all deceitful, so she requested a judgment to dissolve the engagement and return the borrowed money, etc. She then presented the receipt and the false promissory note as evidence, along with a letter in which the defendant boasted that Minister of Finance Kong, Cai Zengji of the Municipal Finance Bureau, former Vice Minister Zheng Hongnian, and the director of the Jiangnan Shipyard could all guarantee him. If the aforementioned individuals could indeed guarantee him, then the matter could be resolved. The court then announced that when the summons for the defendant was delivered to No. 11, Changyuan Lane, Haining Road, North Sichuan Road, it was claimed that he had already left and his whereabouts were unknown. His family had already placed an advertisement in the newspaper to find him, so they refused to accept the summons. She was asked for her opinion on this point, and Miss Tsai stated that this was perhaps a conspiracy between them. Since they refused to accept the summons, she requested that it be served by public notice and that his father, Wang Ruiqing, be summoned to court. Birthday Celebration for Mother; Case of Thugs Extorting Money Concluded; Verdict Scheduled for 2 PM Today

Two petty thugs, Yan Zulai, nicknamed "Holland Water Bottle," 24 years old, residing at No. 14, Yinyu Lane, Eight Immortals Bridge, spend their days loitering at the Xiafei Tea House at No. 34, Avenue Joffre, specializing in extortion. They consider the area around the North and South Zhujia Bridges as their territory, and often issue invitations under false pretenses, collecting gifts and extorting money in various ways. They regard the nearby salted meat shops, brothels, and prostitutes as their prey. If their demands are not met, they take the opportunity to extort money under false pretenses. The victims fear the evil influence of their gang and mostly endure the pain without arguing, aiming to avoid trouble. Recently, on the occasion of Yan's mother's 58th birthday, Yan issued a large number of invitations, scheduling the celebration for his mother's sixtieth birthday on the 26th of this month at the Sanhe Restaurant in Xixinqiao. In addition to issuing invitations to various Korean brothels and prostitutes, he also distributed them to shops in the vicinity. The matter was discovered by Inspector Jin Jiulin of the French Concession Police, who believed that Yan often extorted money under false pretenses, which was a violation of the law. Therefore, at 4 PM on the 26th, he led detectives Zhang Ziying and Dai Rongji to the Sanhe Restaurant, first arresting Luo Weixiang, a native of Ningbo (23 years old, residing at No. 169, Rue Challe, a member of Yan's gang), who was responsible for receiving gifts and keeping accounts for Yan. They also seized a large number of gift registers, gifts, remaining invitations, and thank-you notes. Then, they went to the Xiafei Tea House and arrested Yan, taking him and the others to the police station and sending them to the Second Special Court for interrogation and investigation. This was reported in this newspaper. At 11 AM yesterday, Judge Xiong of the Second Special Court presided over the interrogation in the First Criminal Court. First, lawyer Fei Xizhen from the Police Department explained the case and filed charges of fraud in accordance with Article 339 of the Criminal Code, requesting an investigation and trial. Subsequently, ten witnesses, including the madams of Korean brothels Sun Zhu, Zhang Wang, Wu Zhao, Ma Gao, Lu Mao, Wu Wang, Tang Zhang, Wang Lin, Jin Guiying, Kong Linji, and Hua Jintang, testified one after another, stating that they did not know the defendant. They said that the invitations stated that they should send a gift of two yuan, and they would come to collect it. Some stated that they did not send gifts because they did not know him. When Yan Zulai was interrogated, he claimed that he distributed invitations to celebrate his mother's birthday and did not forcefully extort money. Luo Weixiang testified that Yan invited him to help and he did not dare to extort money with him. Finally, the detectives reported that after arresting the defendant, they investigated the Sanhe Restaurant. According to the owner of the restaurant, the defendant only paid a deposit of two yuan and had not confirmed the number of tables for the banquet, saying that it would be settled after the meal. The court verified the testimonies and ordered the arguments to be concluded, scheduling the verdict to be announced at 2 PM on the 31st (today). The defendants were returned to custody.

Continental Bank Attempts to Cancel Bond Subscription Contracts; Thirteen Banks File a Lawsuit; Lawsuit Filed Against the Bank for Breach of Contract and Payment of Interest; Defendant Claims Contract Should Be Abandoned Due to Government's Unified Issuance Policy

In order to promote the circulation of their banknotes in the market and regulate finance, banks in Shanghai that issue banknotes have entered into bond subscription contracts with general banks and Qian Zhuang that do not have the right to issue banknotes. One party gains the benefit of promoting banknotes, and the other party gains the convenience of business. The term of these contracts is usually three or five years. The subscriber must deposit 40% of the face value in cash with the banknote-issuing bank as a guarantee for the bond subscription, and the banknote-issuing bank must pay interest on the guarantee deposit, usually calculated at an annual rate of 6.5%. However, since the Ministry of Finance implemented currency reform on November 4th of this year,

and the banknotes of the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications were adopted as legal tender, some banknote-issuing banks seized the opportunity to issue circulars to various bond-subscribing banks and Qian Zhuang, intending to cancel the previously signed bond subscription contracts. After deliberation among the banks and Qian Zhuang, they unanimously opposed it. The bank also realized that it lacked a justification and voluntarily abandoned the proposal to cancel the contracts. But one wave had barely subsided before another arose. Now, the Continental Bank is also seeking to cancel such contracts, leading to a lawsuit against it. The Qian Zhuang that have subscribed to bonds from the Continental Bank

include Huafeng, Runfeng, Zhentai, Changshun, Yisheng, Fuchang, Yuzhong, Wanmao, Huatong, Demao, Hengmao, Zhengkang, and Yuanfeng, a total of thirteen Qian Zhuang. The amount of the bonds subscribed is 1.75 million yuan. The interest paid by the Continental Bank on the 40% cash guarantee is 6.5% per annum. After receiving the notice from the Continental Bank, the Qian Zhuang, considering the interests of all bond-subscribing banks and Qian Zhuang, convened a general meeting. They all believed that other banknote-issuing banks had not taken such action, so why should the Continental Bank be different? They then elected representatives Ma Wenxiang, Liu Ximeng, Yin Huanzhi, and others to negotiate with Ye Fuxiao, the president of the Continental Bank, demanding that the contract be upheld and that the thirteen Qian Zhuang be paid the

interest of 60,000 yuan. Because they were refused, the Qian Zhuang jointly hired lawyer Zhan Jifeng to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Local Court against the Continental Bank and its president, Ye Fuxiao, for breach of contract and payment of interest. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Daxi opened the court for hearing. Lawyer Zhan stated that all the plaintiffs had signed contracts with the defendant to promote the sale of banknotes. In order to ensure the stability of issuance, the Ministry of Finance ordered the banknote-issuing banks to deposit a guarantee deposit with the Central Bank and pay interest on the guarantee deposit. Therefore, the defendant should also pay interest on the guarantee deposit received from the plaintiffs. However, the defendant is using the government's

currency reform as an excuse to cancel the signed bond subscription contracts and stop paying interest. However, currency reform is one thing, and the bond subscription contract is another. How can the currency reform affect the validity of the contract? Moreover, the interest paid by the Central Bank to the defendant is more favorable than the interest paid by the defendant to the plaintiffs. Since the Central Bank has not stopped paying interest on the guarantee deposit paid by the defendant, the defendant cannot stop paying interest to the plaintiffs. The matter is clear. Therefore, the plaintiffs request a judgment that the contract

continues to be valid and that the interest owed by the defendant, up to tomorrow (31st), should be paid immediately, and that the litigation costs should be borne by the defendant. The defendant's lawyer argued that the government's centralized reserve and unified issuance policy constitutes a "special event" as stipulated in the contract. Therefore, the defendant proposes to abandon the contract because, according to the order of the Ministry of Finance, in addition to the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, new banknotes from other banks with the right to issue banknotes will no longer be issued, and the old banknotes that have been issued will also be gradually recalled. Therefore, the lawyers of both parties argued about whether the currency reform constitutes a "special event" in the contract. The court also believed that this issue requires careful consideration and ordered both parties to withdraw and wait for a postponed hearing.

Two Japanese in Straits Due to Poverty; One Attempts Suicide by Disembowelment, One by Hanging; Takashima Nijiji's Life May Be Saved, Akiyama Tokisuke Has Already Died

According to the Japanese-language Shanghai Daily, Takashima Nijiji, 47 years old, from Ishikawa County, Fukushima Prefecture, Japan, came to Shanghai in 1923 to run an antique business. He resided in a room on the second floor of the home of Koike Tsukasa at No. 160, Rue Maignan. Due to recent business failures and being pressured by poverty, he suddenly used a kitchen knife to disembowel himself deep in the night of the 28th. It was not until the 29th that the neighbors in the back room heard moaning and, peering through the window, saw blood on the bedding. They urgently reported to the Hino Hospital, which sent a doctor to treat him. After bandaging the 20 cm incision below the navel, they telegraphed the Consulate General Police Department, which sent him to the Fumin Hospital. After a detailed examination, it was discovered that there were also knife wounds on both sides of the neck. Although the neck had been repeatedly cut, the abdominal cavity had not been reached, so there was no danger to his life.

According to the Mainichi Shimbun, Akiyama Tokisuke from Kyoto County, Fukuoka Prefecture, resided at the home of Iho Jutaro in the Zhonghe Building at No. 293, Avenue Edward VII. In August of this year, he served as the supervisor of the Towa-kan construction site. Since October, due to poor capital management, the employer has stopped paying wages, leaving him without food expenses. He then had suicidal thoughts. He reported it to the Japanese Consulate Police Department, which brought Dr. Tonimiya from Fumin Hospital to examine the scene. The result was that the estimated time of death was more than 30 hours.

China Bank Inspection Report

The 94th inspection report of the Shanghai China Bank Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states: In accordance with the rules, this committee inspected the issuance of the Shanghai China Bank, the reserve vault for the exchange coupons used by its branches and various firms. On December 29th, the 24th year of the Republic of China, Dai Mingli, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, Wang Yansong and Pei Yunqing, representatives of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Peishen and Hu Xiqian, representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association, Liu Wuqiao and Zhang Wenbo, representatives of the Shanghai Money Trade Association, Xu Maotang and Shen Jingliang, representatives of the various firms redeeming the coupons, and Zhou Zongliang, Wang Baolun, and Lu Jianquan, representatives of the bank's directors and supervisors, together with accountant Wang Zikang, held the 94th inspection at the bank. The results of the inspection are listed as follows: Total amount of exchange coupon issuance: 17,566,7224 yuan, including: 11,151,8264 yuan issued by the bank, 49,133,965 yuan used by its branches, and 15,014,995 yuan used by various firms. Total amount of exchange coupon reserve: 17,566,7224 yuan, including cash reserve of 12,902,5598 yuan, 2 jiao, 3 fen, and guarantee reserve of 4,664,1625 yuan, 7 jiao, 7 fen. The above cash reserve accounts for 60%, and the guarantee reserve accounts for 40%. All were accurately checked. This is a formal report. December 29th, 24th year of the Republic of China.
