Educational News

Shanghai Municipal High School and Normal School Graduation Joint Examination Temporarily Postponed: Graduating Students Examined on Dates Designated by Schools, and the Education Bureau Must Be Notified in Advance for Dispatch of Proctors; Students Taking Make-Up Exams from Other Provinces Will Participate in the Make-Up Exams in the Next Semester

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has decided to temporarily postpone the joint examinations for high schools, normal schools, and physical education normal schools this semester because the summer vacation for secondary schools in the city has been advanced, and the dates of the winter vacation vary from school to school. Students taking make-up exams will be postponed to the next semester. Instructions and announcements were issued separately yesterday, as follows:

Joint Graduation Examination Temporarily Postponed

Yesterday, the Municipal Education Bureau issued instructions to public and private high schools, normal schools, and physical education normal schools in the city, stating that according to regulations, graduating students of high schools, normal schools, and physical education normal schools should take the graduation joint examination from January 6th to 8th next year. However, since the summer vacation has been advanced this year and the winter vacation dates vary from school to school, it is difficult to hold the joint examination. With the approval of the Ministry of Education, all kinds of joint examinations this semester will be temporarily postponed. All schools that have already reported graduating students should designate the dates for the graduation examination and report them to the bureau in advance so that personnel can be dispatched to the school to proctor the examination carefully. This order must be complied with.

Students Taking Make-Up Exams Will Participate in the Next Semester

In addition, the Municipal Education Bureau announced yesterday that the joint graduation examination for high schools, normal schools, and physical education normal schools this semester has been temporarily postponed because the summer vacation has been advanced this year and the winter vacation dates vary from school to school, making it difficult to hold the joint examination. With the approval of the Ministry of Education, all students in this city who failed one or two subjects in the graduation joint examination and students from other provinces who were entrusted to take the make-up examination will be postponed to the next semester's joint examination for make-up exams. In addition to replying by letter, this announcement is hereby made known to all.

Cultural Construction Association Reading Competition Examination: To Be Held Simultaneously in Various Places Starting January 3rd; The Examination Location in This City is Borrowed from the Youth High School

Since the organization of the reading competition hosted by the Chinese Cultural Construction Association, no less than 10,000 people have registered to participate in various places. Now the first exam will be held for three days, and the examination location and schedule in this city have been set. Details are as follows:

To Be Held Simultaneously in Various Places

The examination date is from January 3rd for three days, and will be held simultaneously in various counties and cities. No early start is allowed. All teachers' questions should be based on the question-and-answer method, with textbooks accounting for 80% and reference books accounting for 20%. Standard answers and scoring methods shall be formulated by the question setters. All matters shall be organized and prepared by the examination committee organized by the general association. After the examinations in various places, the general association will select the ten best students in the university group and the high school group to hold a re-examination at a specific location to determine the ranking of the top ten.

Examination Schedule for This City

The examination location for reading members of the Shanghai Branch will be borrowed from the Youth High School on Xiafei Road. The schedule is as follows: January 3rd, Party Doctrine from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM, Philosophy from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM (Logic for the high school group), Economics for the university group from 3:30 PM to 5:30 PM. January 4th, Natural Science from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM, Politics from 1:00 PM to 4:00 PM. January 5th, History from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM, Geography from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM. Candidates should bring their admission tickets and membership cards when entering the examination hall.

Regulations from the Municipal Education Bureau on Changing the Start and End Dates of the Winter Vacation for Secondary and Higher Education Institutions This Year: Two Measures Prescribed; All Schools Notified to Comply and Report

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau announced: According to the telegram from the Ministry of Education, local authorities have recently telegraphed to request that the start and end dates of the winter vacation for secondary and higher education institutions this year be changed. It is now revised that the winter vacation for secondary and higher education institutions under the bureau will begin on January 4th of the 25th year and end on January 30th. If it is intended to continue the vacation according to the regulations on January 18th, the bureau may handle it according to the actual situation, etc. In compliance with this, two measures are now formulated: (1) Advance the winter vacation, and all examination matters must be completed within two weeks after the start of the second semester. (2) Do not advance the winter vacation, and continue the vacation according to the regulations on January 18th. After the end of the annual vacation, classes and examinations must be conducted as usual, and the principal must be absolutely responsible for the students' actions. All public and private secondary and higher education institutions in this city may handle the above two measures at their own discretion and report to the bureau for record. This is hereby announced.

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau instructed the private Huanghuagang High School: According to the case, the school has repeatedly been ordered by the bureau to comply with the Ministry's order to convert to an industrial vocational school. A directive from the Ministry of Education, Pu Jiu Er No. 12030, has been received, approving the proposed handling of the case. The school should be closed for rectification. You should comply with the Ministry's order." The school is hereby ordered to promptly close and cease operations before the end of this semester and report for verification. Do not violate this order.

Jiangwan Cross-Country Race to Be Held on January 5th

The Chinese Athletic Association's Track and Field Team is organizing the Jiangwan Six-Mile Cross-Country Race, scheduled to start at 9:30 AM on January 5th next month at the side gate of Hongkou Park's west entrance. Details have already been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the route for this race has been mapped out by General Secretary Sun Zhi, and staff have been appointed. As of yesterday, twenty-seven racers have registered to participate. Mr. Li Yagu is requesting Liang Saihu to provide awards.

Racers:

(Open Group) Zhou Ruquan, Qiu Zongcheng, Li Hui, Gu Weiyuan, He Baoshan, Bao Yibi, Lin Quanbo, Zhou Zhicheng, Li Qingji, Chen Zongqi, Lu Shuiqi, Lü Jinming. Route:

Starting from the west side gate of Hongkou Park, proceed along Jiangwan Road to the Hongkou Swimming Pool, then turn into East Sports Association Road, cross the wooden bridge approximately one hundred feet north, turn right onto the gravel road, then through rural field paths to the vicinity of the Nursery Stock Company, enter Xiangyin Road, head west, then re-enter East Sports Association Road, proceed south, cross the wooden bridge again, pass the Hongkou Swimming Pool, enter Jiangwan Road, and enter the west side gate of Hongkou Park to reach the finish line. Colored paper scraps will be placed along the route for racers to follow.

Notice:

Racers' Notice: (1) Racers must report near the bungalow at the west side gate inside Hongkou Park at 8:30 AM on the morning of the race to collect their number cloth. (2) The race starts at 9:30 AM; latecomers will not be waited for. (3) Substitution by another person is strictly prohibited.

National Sports Basketball to Arrive in Shanghai Soon

According to Li Zhenzhong, the National Sports team's trip to the South Seas is entirely educational in nature. Since the team members will all graduate next summer, this trip can serve as both a tour and a skill exploration, as well as demonstrate the level of domestic basketball technology to overseas Chinese. The group of seven includes team leader Pang Yusen and team members Zhang Changjiang, Zhang Changqing, Gao Changming, Wu Wenzhong, Tang Shikun, and Li Zhenzhong. They are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai before January 5th to await passage abroad, departing on the President Dollar liner no later than the 6th or 7th. Principal Zhang Zhijiang, who has returned from a tour of Europe, is scheduled to arrive in Singapore on January 7th and plans to wait for the entire team to arrive in Singapore to join them on their southern expedition. The team plans to go directly to Singapore without stopping in Hong Kong. It is estimated that there will be four games in Singapore, then on to Malaysia, Java, Penang, and finally the Philippines. The match arrangements along the way will be handled by Principal Zhang, but have not yet been finalized. They are scheduled to leave the Philippines in early March and return directly to Shanghai.

Unable to Participate in World Games Selection

Mr. Li also said that the National Sports team will not be able to participate in the World Games selection, which will be held in Shanghai at the end of January. According to Li, the World Games selection was originally scheduled to take place in mid-March. However, Principal Zhang was in the midst of finalizing the details of the National Sports team's trip to the South Seas, when they were suddenly notified that the selection would be held earlier, at the end of January. In fact, it would be impossible to do both. However, to maintain credibility with overseas Chinese, the trip to the South Seas cannot be cancelled. The Athletic Association, which is in charge of the selection, does not yet have a proper solution. In my opinion, it would be best to hold the preliminary selection at the end of January and then hold the final selection in March. This approach is somewhat biased. I believe that General Secretary Shen will have a satisfactory solution. What I have said is just a personal hope.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Boy (140)

— Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

The little house’s value increased quickly. Soon he was quite satisfied with this investment and planned to use the principal to buy unheard-of treasures. He recorded each deposit. Aunt Guang Sheng allowed him to wait until his savings reached five yuan, and then he could buy eggs. He was overjoyed and ran to the barn, took out the four shiny, large-sized silver dollar coins, and showed them to Naide.

Naide looked at them, expressing extreme envy, and said, "It's a pity I don't have that much, otherwise, combined with my accumulated three yuan, it would be almost enough to buy the violin I've longed for for so long."

"Maybe I can lend you some. I haven't decided how to use my money yet," said, while tossing his silver coins and catching them again with his hand.

Suddenly, someone shouted from behind the warehouse, "Hey, kids, come to the river to see Dunn catch a live, big snake."

"Let's go," said. He casually threw the money into an old grain cleaner and ran off in a puff of smoke, followed by Naide.

Securities Market

**Public Bonds: Major Players Attempt Sophistication, Retail Investors Deceived, Most Bonds Fall, Few Rise**

Yesterday, the Chinese Merchants Stock Exchange saw quite lively trading. Major short sellers deliberately created confusion, pretending to exit but actually increasing positions to mislead observers. Simultaneously, they entrusted other brokers to sell off, while individual retail investors were uniformly deceived. Since rumors of interest rate cuts spread in the market, confidence has gradually weakened. Furthermore, following the sharp decline in silver prices, financial institutions rushed to convert foreign exchange into local currency, forcing them to sell bonds to compensate. Previously, they bought bonds and sold foreign exchange; now, they are doing the opposite, following the same pattern. The difference in actions caused extreme market volatility. In the afternoon, rumors of Japanese yen transactions further destabilized the market. As predicted the previous day, yesterday's trading was undoubtedly small due to the aforementioned reasons. The future remains turbulent. Yesterday's trading involved three sessions, starting weak but strengthening before a final surge of over one yuan, leading many to believe a rebound was imminent. However, unbeknownst to them, while No. 54 heavily absorbed bonds, they were simultaneously selling off large quantities on the other side, misleading those who further fueled the surge. This could be seen from the second session onwards, where No. 54 immediately began selling off, causing the market price to drop by several jiao (tenths of a yuan) to over one yuan. Selling pressure remained strong during the afternoon session, causing a further decline of about half a yuan. Throughout the day, Nos. 32, 48, and 78 consistently sold off. Buying interest was scattered. As a result, apart from 19, 22, and 96, which performed well, rising five fen (hundredths of a yuan) to four jiao and a half, the rest uniformly fell, ranging from two or three jiao to nine jiao. Yarn and Cotton

**Monthly Yarn and Cotton Delivery Review**

Yarn Price: 200 yuan - Volume: 13,800 bales

Cotton Price: 41.5 yuan - Volume: 85,400 dan (approximately 50 kg)

The Jin Jin Ji brand of yarn for December delivery was launched on July 1st of this year at a price of 169 yuan, followed by 169.7 yuan. Subsequently, due to the unrest in North China, sluggish yarn sales, tight credit, and large-scale selling by Japanese merchants, the pressure was severe. By July 13th, the near-month contract broke the 60-yuan mark, with a low of 165.2 yuan. Later, due to the difficult operating conditions of yarn mills, coupled with hot weather, more and more factories suspended or reduced production, leading to a reduction in output. At the same time, margin calls trended higher, and some speculators actively purchased. Rumors of severe currency problems circulated, causing the market to turn from weak to strong. By July 30th, the price jumped five yuan in one day, and cotton rose 1.3 yuan, reaching a high of 179.7 yuan. The high price hindered actual sales, and customer demand was subdued, causing the market to be controlled. By August 28th, the price had fallen again to [blank] yuan, followed by a long period of sideways movement. By October, margin call increases became more pronounced, and market prices steadily advanced, reaching new highs, breaking through the 1,200 yuan level. Financial institutions and certain entrusted parties eagerly absorbed, rushing in like swarms of bees, causing prices to surge from the 70 yuan level to 198 yuan, with minor fluctuations along the way. On November 4th, the National Government announced that the banknotes of the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications were legal tender, further fueling market frenzy. Prices jumped 10 yuan in one session, reaching 204 yuan. At this time, rumors spread in the local market, and profitable longs exited, dropping the price below 191.9 yuan. However, banks, gold merchants, and public bond traders continued to buy, taking a bullish view on margin yarn, absorbing contracts with distant delivery dates in substantial amounts, and consistently refusing to release them. This resulted in an increasing gap between near- and far-month contracts, prompting arbitrage activity. Therefore, although sellers diligently pressured prices and actively delivered goods, arbitrageurs swept them up. In recent days, the price has broken through the 200 yuan level again, reaching 202 yuan. The final session price was 201 yuan, up 3.5 yuan from the previous month. The delivery price for three days was set at 200 yuan, with a remaining balance of 13,800 bales. New goods delivered included 2,000 bales of Kuei Hsing No. 2, 1,00 yuan of Da Fa, 1,400 bales of Jin Jin Ji, 1,050 bales of Shuang Ma, 800 bales of Tian Guan, 500 bales of Xing Shi, 350 bales of Shuang Lu, 100 bales of Di Qiu, 150 bales of Kong Que, 350 bales of Hong Fu, 550 bales of Jin Ta, 300 bales of San Xing, and 1,000 bales of Qi Qiu, totaling 9,500 bales. The rest were self-delivered. The China Cotton Corporation received 2,000 bales, a certain company received 5,500 bales, and arbitrageurs accounted for the majority. Grains

**Ke Xian Rice Arrives in Force, Sales are Lackluster**

Yesterday, the Ke Xian rice market saw a surge in arrivals, with whole shipments from Anqing, Wenzhou, Taizhou, and Shaoxing arriving in port. However, sales were limited to local buyers, further weakening the market. Consequently, sellers were willing to lower prices to offload their stocks, and prices fell slightly by three to five fen. Yesterday and the day before, 400 tons were traded at a price of 11.8 yuan. Yesterday, another 300 tons were traded at a price of 11.75 yuan, all of which were contracted for delivery in January and February. The changes in the overall trend depend on the opening of the new year. The present-day hairy flax also softened, leading to no transactions.

Special Article

**China's Tea Industry (4)**

*Yi Bai*

In Jiangxi Province, with the exception of the Zhen Zhi Company, which uses machinery, all green tea is roasted by hand, and the method is roughly similar to that of Anhui and Zhejiang. The Jiangxi Tea Zhen Zhi Co., Ltd. is one of the few tea factories in China. It was established in the fourth year of the Republic of China with a capital of 130,000 yuan. It is located in Taixiang, east of Xiushui City, and has its own tea garden of 2,595 mu. The machinery used for kneading tea was originally nine Jacprons Rapid Roller type kneading machines manufactured by Japan. Subsequently, due to poor performance, four Indian-style tea kneading machines were purchased from the United Kingdom. However, the tea roasting utensils still use the old method of roasting.

(Fujian) Fujian produces a lot of tea, and its products are sold in Southeast Asia. However, due to the import of Taiwanese white tea to Shantou and other ports, the Chinese tea market in Southeast Asia has been encroached upon, and it has been decreasing year by year. The tea making methods in Fujian are all old-fashioned manual methods, the same as those in Jiangxi, Anhui, and Zhejiang.

(Hunan and Hubei) The number of tea-producing families in the two lakes is the highest in the country. In the past, more than 400,000 boxes were exported every year. Recently, because the tea-producing areas in Hunan and Hubei have been occupied by the communist bandits, and because of tight money and sluggish exports, the tea industry has plummeted. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, 610,000 dan of Chinese tea were exported from Hankou, but by the 19th year, it had fallen to 310,000 dan. There are four brick tea factories in Hankou, three of which are owned by Russian merchants and one by Chinese merchants. Later, because the Russian merchant factories dumped Soviet tea and the Soviet Union restricted Chinese tea, one factory was closed and one was sold off in the 11th year of the [blank]. The Chinese Commercial Brick Factory is an outstanding brick tea factory in China. It was founded in the 32nd year of Guangxu in the Qing Dynasty with a capital of 500,000 yuan. The products include rice brick tea, red brick tea, and green brick tea. Its quality is relatively good. Unfortunately, it was flooded during the great flood in 1932, causing great damage. Although it was restored later, it also encountered the Sino-Japanese Incident and economic panic, so it is still in a critical situation.

(Jiangsu) Jiangsu tea has suffered a devastating blow from competition with Japanese tea in recent years. According to a survey report, there are a total of 85 tea factories in the province. However, the largest capital is only 15,000 yuan, and only 14 companies have it. The scale is very small, and production is carried out in handicraft mode. (The tea conditions in each province are based on the economic yearbook of the Ministry of Industry)

From this point of view, Chinese tea should not be able to compete with emerging tea-producing countries in the world. For example, China's tea-making machines still need to be purchased from Japan and India, which are backward tea-producing countries. There is no improvement. In addition, the quantity of machines purchased from backward countries is negligible, which is the biggest proof that Chinese tea cannot be developed. This situation is like the Sino-Japanese War in Gubeikou, where China fought against Japan's 20th-century airplanes and tanks with 18th-century broadswords. As a result, China was at a disadvantage.

5. Preliminary Views on the Improvement Plan of Chinese Tea Production and Sales

Although Chinese tea has been competed by emerging tea-producing countries and is in a desperate situation, China is still the kingdom of tea-producing countries in the world in terms of quantity. According to the tea industry in the economics dictionary published by the Japanese Reform Agency: in 1928, the total world tea production was 4,700,100 tons, and China accounted for 6% and 7% of its 3 million tons. According to the survey of the Economic Research Office of the Bank of China, the annual output of Chinese tea is 7.9 million city dans. According to the total production of tea-producing countries in the world (excluding China) in 1933, 4,090,495 hectoliters, which is equivalent to 8,180,990 city dans, China's output accounts for more than 49% of the world's output. Since China has such a huge amount of tea production, if it can scientifically improve its quality and make its transportation and sales mechanism sound, then there is no reason for Chinese tea to decline. The details are as follows:

First, the urgent need for improvement on the tea industry itself

A. Tea planting mountains should be improved

Chinese farmers are often conservative. According to the "Shishi News" on September 14th of this year: "The tea-producing area in Longjing, Hangzhou, covers an area of more than 100 mu and produces more than 100 dan every year. - Recently, inchworms have been found, which are extremely harmful and have been ineffective in killing them. The green leaves on all the tea trees in Longjing have been eaten, leaving only dead branches standing, like after a fire. The spread is so fast that the nearby Wengjiashan and Yangjiashan areas have been affected, and the area affected by the insect disaster has extended to about 1,000 mu. Production is hopeless next year." This situation is caused by the neglect of scientific management by tea planters. According to a letter from the Shanghai Tea Association to the National Economic Commission, in the item "Improvement of Production," it is briefly stated that the production of tea in Xiushui County and/or [blank] is extremely [blank]. During the most prosperous period of the year, the annual output was 180,000 boxes, but now it is less than 10,000 boxes, because the tea land has been left barren due to sluggish exports. It is urgent to provide relief. The method of relief is: loosening the soil, weeding, replanting, and fertilizing. For example, every autumn, dig up the soil in the tea planting mountains, remove weeds, and apply a little fertilizer, such as leaf fertilizer and soybean cake. Remove old tea trees and replant new ones. As for insect pests, drugs that do not harm the tea trees can be used to repel them.

B. Tea making technology should be modernized and industrialized

At present, Chinese tea production is still done by hand, which is not suitable for the 20th century. Because Chinese tea relies on sunlight exposure, it often has a bad smell. Even unscientific iron pot roasting is difficult to obtain good tea flavor. If all the production tools of Chinese tea are replaced by modern machines, the absorption of tea moisture can be limited to a certain extent, and the color and taste of tea can be retained to a certain extent. There is no phenomenon of excessive fermentation or uneven color and taste. The reason why tea from India, Japan, and Ceylon can gain market share is that the modernization and industrialization of tea production. What should be avoided most is that Chinese tea merchants value short-term benefits and forget permanent interests. For example, tea leaves are mixed with tea stems, artificial colors are dyed in the tea, or water is splashed into the tea leaves. Regarding tea containing moisture, the Ministry of Industry has recently issued an order to ban the sale of all raw tea containing more than 45% moisture. However, it is best for tea merchants to realize this themselves. This is no different from a moth seeing fire as light, but in reality, it is suicide. The quality of Chinese tea is superior to that of the rest of the world due to the relationship between the [blank] of the land, as mentioned above. Therefore, Chinese tea can still be sold to tea-producing countries such as India and Japan. The high-quality tea in these tea-producing countries still needs to be mixed with Chinese tea. If Chinese tea makers can implement large-scale modern industrialization with a long-term vision, the future of Chinese tea will still be infinitely bright. (To be continued)

Eating in Shanghai

— Zhu Ying

That's why Shanghai has all kinds of tastes. Now let's talk about restaurants.

There are tropical Indian restaurants and frigid Russian restaurants. Oriental cuisine and Western white cuisine are all available.

As for domestic restaurants, there are even more. Beijing, Tianjin, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Fujian, Hangzhou, Su Bang, and Yang Bang, there are too many to count. In particular, Guangdong restaurants, Hui restaurants, Ningbo gangs and Wuxi gangs, and local restaurants are everywhere. In addition, there are Qingzhen sects and Buddhist vegetarian restaurants. Some people say that only rich people can afford to eat in these restaurants. That's right. But peddlers and pawns also have a place to enjoy themselves, because in Shanghai, in the slums, there are always a few small restaurants on every street that sell cheap dishes. To be more economical, beggars can also taste delicious food for two or three cents. However, what they taste is not a bowl of dishes, but the leftovers from big restaurants pieced together.

Songjiang Four-Gilled Perch

— Jia Chengsheng

Time flies like running water. In the blink of an eye, it's mid-winter again. In this cold and snowy weather, the famous Songjiang four-gilled perch has become a seasonal food and a treasure for banquets.

Songjiang perch does not have any special taste, but it has been handed down to this day because it has been sung by poets.

Although there is more than one area in Songjiang that produces perch, perch is divided into three-gilled and four-gilled, with the four-gilled being more valuable. It is produced in a pool of clear water under Xiuye Bridge in Songcheng, and the output is the least. Although the output of other places is large, they are all three-gilled.

When perch first came on the market, four-gilled sold for one yuan a catty, and three-gilled can get two to three catties, the cheapest being four catties for one yuan.

There is no fixed price for eating a hot pot of perch in a restaurant in Songjiang City. It depends on how many people eat. For example, if four people eat, two tails per person, with three or four other foods, such as chicken slices, meat slices, and winter bamboo shoots, the initial market price is about 1.6 yuan, and after a long time, it will be 1.2 yuan.

If you need perch for a family banquet, you must order it from the fish shop one or two days in advance, otherwise it will not be available at that time, because four-gilled perch is only produced under Xiuye Bridge, and the daily supply is less than the demand.

Perch dies when it is out of the water, and it has the same characteristics as [blank] fish, so it is difficult to carry to other places. This may be one of the reasons why it is so valuable. If there is train transportation between Beijing, Shanghai, and Hangzhou, you can arrive in the morning and afternoon, and many people come to buy it. The way to carry it is to put the fish in bran skin to keep it fresh and not to spoil the taste.

The taste of perch lies in its freshness and tenderness, so its eating method must be raw, just like eating pheasant meat, and the main cooking method must be accompanied by chicken soup and winter bamboo shoots.

Pudong in Shanghai also produces perch, and the output is very large, but they are three-gilled, which are regarded as ordinary things in the market, and the price is also cheap. In fact, the freshness and tenderness are better than Songjiang perch, and those who like fresh food can also try it.

Dongshan Mutton

— Zhu Shaofei

It's the season for mutton to be on the market again. On every street, in front of small tea houses and noodle shops, you can see mutton vendors parked. Green, dried lotus leaves loosely cover slices of white meat. A serving costs three or four hundred coppers. Go to a noodle shop for a bowl of plain noodles, or to a tea house for fifty coppers worth of old wheat wine. Put your feet up, take a sip of wine, pick up a slice of meat with your fingers, and leisurely chat with people. During this time of year, if you don't indulge in this, you're considered unsophisticated.

Chapter 22: A Knight's Words Move Painted Lips, a Fair Maiden Plots, False Affection Startles a Jade Wrist, a Suffering Woman Flees Imprisonment

Mrs. Zhou said, "Ms. Zhu, if you don't dare to go home, I have an idea. You can move upstairs and live in the room next to Mrs. Lan. No matter what, don't come out. If he doesn't ask us for you, we'll demand an explanation from him. If he comes to find us, that's even better. We'll throw him out of this hotel, and then it's done. You just hide, even if the sky falls, there's a roof to hold it up. What are you afraid of?" Yueying leaned against a pillar in the hall, twisting a corner of her clothing in her hand and biting it with her mouth. She lowered her head, looking at her toes, pondering this problem. Mrs. Liu pushed her, saying, "Why are you so excessively timid? With so many of us helping you, what are you afraid of? If you live next to Mrs. Lan, he'll find Mrs. Lan first if he comes looking for you. Mrs. Lan can send him away. In broad daylight, under the bright sky, no one can eat a person alive. Your suffering is truly enough for anyone to bear. No wonder you cried." She held Yueying's hand and walked upstairs, chattering incessantly. However, Wang Beihai, who was watching from downstairs, was mesmerized. He pressed his hands on the table, half-raised his body, neither standing nor sitting, just staring at the top of the stairs. Only when Yueying had entered the room did he turn his head, only to see Jia Duocai walking in from outside with a stern face and swaying gait. He seemed to have thought of something at the entrance screen, and paused for a moment. Later, seeing the group of older women in the reception hall crowding into the living room, he thought it was an opportunity and immediately ran towards his own room. Ten. A nose can smell bad odors. What if...?

Mutton's main source is a village south of Daishui called Wujia Village. Dozens of families in the village rely on sheep for a living. Except in winter, Dongshan sheep farmers shear wool; in winter, they carry mutton. Their livelihood depends on sheep. Few people raise sheep, but these days, dozens of large merino sheep are slaughtered in the village every day. They come from sheep traders from southern Zhejiang and the Taihu River estuaries. One boatload is sold off, and another arrives at the village.

Each mutton vendor can make three or four hundred yuan in a winter. The business is so large because they allow credit. If you go to the market every day, they'll keep a tab for you. So some households have debts of ten or so yuan by the end of the year. Some even avoid going to the market to evade their mutton debt. So on New Year's Eve, there are scenes of people trying to collect mutton debts, stripping clothes, and blocking doors.

Carrying mutton is the most laborious. They slaughter during the day and set off with their loads at dawn. The farthest they go is across Xiajiao Ridge to Baisha, north of the town. To get to the back of our mountain, they have to pass through Ganshan Ridge, Tangshou Ridge, and reach Yangwan Village, climbing mountains and crossing ridges with heavy loads over these rugged hills and through many villages.

It is said that their method of cooking mutton using fire sounds very strange. They only use a stove of rice straw, simmering the mutton in a pot. At dawn, they remove the bones, transfer the meat to the carrying tray, and set off with it.

Changzhou Steamed Pork with Wine Lees

— Jiao Xin

Our hometown, Changzhou, can be said to produce nothing special. The bamboo combs, once famous throughout the country, are now declining because the manufacturers stick to old methods and are resistant to change. Moreover, in recent years, women have been cutting off their long hair, so bamboo combs are not as necessary as before.

However, there is one food item that goes unnoticed – steamed pork with wine lees – which is now highly praised by everyone. Locals certainly like it, and people from other places who have tasted it will always remember and praise it. Every Lunar New Year, it is an essential delicacy for every household. I heard that someone in Shanghai has already started selling it this year, but because of the ineffective publicity, not many people know about it. I am now writing down its method below to inform those from other places who want to eat it again but do not know how it is made.

Buy a piece of streaky pork from the butcher, cut it into four-inch squares, put it in a pot and add soy sauce and wine (a little, to remove the fishy smell) and boil until cooked. Remove it, let it cool, and then cut it into thin slices of two inches. Apply a little of the coloring sold in soy sauce shops to the skin of the pork (to give it a reddish color, you can skip this step). Place the pork skin down in a coarse rice bowl, and then cover it with aged wine lees (available at distilleries. Before using the lees, stir-fry them slightly in a pot, remove the hard chunks, and add sugar and soy sauce and other seasonings). Add a slice of ginger and a scallion knot on top of the lees, and steam over water four or five times. When eating, pour it into a serving bowl, so that the pork is on top and the lees are on the bottom.

The method of making steamed pork with wine lees is not difficult, and the cost is not expensive. For one yuan, you can make five or six bowls. Its charm lies in its richness without being greasy, its fragrant and rich aroma, and its tenderness like tofu. Even people who don't usually eat fatty meat can eat a slice or two.

Nourishment for the Common People

As the season turns to winter, very affordable nourishing foods become popular as a way for ordinary people to replenish their bodies. Besides preparing them as common side dishes, such as bagged egg, steamed egg, egg dumplings, and egg skin, eating one or two eggs beaten into rice porridge or mixed with white sugar every morning has a considerable nourishing effect on the body.

However, besides the above methods of eating, there is also a method of artificial cultivation, and once cultivated, its nourishing effect is even greater. Prepare fifty or sixty eggs and red dates each. Place each egg inside a red date and bury them separately in the soil on the day of the Winter Solstice (each one must be buried individually). Wait until the day of the Spring Equinox, then dig them out. Take one or two each day with boiled water, which has the effect of replenishing essence and benefiting the body.

Cantonese Three-Snake Stew

— Zhuo

It is now deep winter, which is also the season for Cantonese people to eat three-snake stew. The Cantonese restaurants on North Sichuan Road slaughter large snakes and hang the snake skins in glass window cabinets as signs. Countless pedestrians crane their necks every day to look inside, so at this time and place, you can know what is going on. I eat snake three or four times a year, so I know quite a bit about the taste, and the responsibility of introducing it is unavoidable.

When did eating snake start? How did it develop? What is the reason? Forgive me for not having a historical interest, so I cannot clearly research it. I only ate it because I was greedy, following other people. That was more than ten years ago, in our hometown... Guangdong. The so-called three snakes are three kinds of snakes called "golden leg band," "over-tree banyan," and "finger snapper." Why these three kinds of snakes are mixed together to eat, I also don't understand. In fact, it's not necessarily that these three kinds of snakes have to be combined to be delicious, because their tastes are not different at all. As for whether this is more beneficial to the body, it's a bit mystical.

The cooking method for snake, according to my experience, is always the same. The snake is slaughtered, the skin is removed, and then the meat and skin are put into a pot and boiled until cooked. Then it is taken out and shredded like eel, and the skin is also cut into thin strips (some methods don't use the skin, but I think the skin mixed in with the meat strips has a special flavor, because the skin curls up when cooked, like eating snail meat, which is crisp). Then it is mixed with civet cat, hawk, abalone, shiitake mushrooms, pig tongue, etc., which are cut or shredded, and put into a pot together and simmered for two or three hours, then it can be eaten. Snake meat is already very fresh and sweet, and with the addition of so many meats and vegetables, it tastes even more delicious, rich, smooth, and palatable. Because so many things are mixed together, the true taste of the snake is actually not easy to distinguish. Even the snake meat strips must be carefully identified to be seen. I think this pot of meat stew would be very good even without snake meat in it. It is said that snake bile is most beneficial to the human body (whether this is true remains to be investigated), so when slaughtering the snake, the gallbladder is carefully extracted first, and then the bile is mixed into the wine, which is called "snake bile wine." It has a slight cool taste when you drink it, which is quite interesting.

It is said that snake scales and bones are poisonous, and it is not fun to eat them by mistake, so when shredding the snake meat, you have to be very careful. This work is probably not very difficult, as we have never heard of any accidents happening because of this. It is also said by those who are experienced in eating snake that it is forbidden to have sexual relations after eating snake, otherwise the children born will grow skin like snake scales. So whenever eating snake, you will always hear such words: "Behave yourself tonight, be careful of raising a child with snake scales." Whether this statement is superstitious, I do not know, because there has been no experimental report. However, this matter is always inappropriate after being drunk and full, and perhaps the intention of the elders lies in this.

The Year's Summary

— Meng Ruo

1935 will soon become a page in history. Here I will list a few major events that happened in the world and in China this year as a summary of the year.

The most shocking event in the world this year was the East African War. In the development of this war, one side, the aggressor, unleashed its ambition to swallow the weak, while the other side, the oppressed, insisted on its determination to resist power. On the other hand, Britain and France first implemented sanctions against Italy, and then advocated auctioning off Abyssinia. Currently, the war between the two countries is still in a stalemate, and the resolution of the Italian-Abyssinian issue in the future is unlikely to be achieved by any peaceful solution.

Secondly, the naval conference currently being held in London is also worth mentioning. The holding of this conference is only to do what one can, and there is little hope of success. The naval competition between Britain, the United States, and Japan has become increasingly acute, and compromise is by no means easy. However, the success or failure of this conference is of great importance to the Far Eastern issue. As the center of the Far Eastern issue, China has a need to pay full attention.

Speaking of our country, in this year, external pressure has only aggravated our difficulties. The twenty-two counties of eastern Hebei have been controlled by traitors, and the two provinces of Hebei and Chahar have also formed a disguised autonomous region. Recently, there has been a rumor of Inner Mongolia declaring independence, and the news of the loss of Guyuan. All of these can ruin the country's vitality. Therefore, the work of saving the country and preserving its existence in the future cannot be shouldered solely by the national people, I fear there will be no day to save the national fortunes.

Looking at the above, the world in 1935 was a time when the strong intensified the seizure of colonies. This phenomenon is the result of the development of imperialism. Now that 1935 is about to end, what follows is the crisis-ridden 1936. The future of the world will enter a great era in history. In this era, the iron hooves of the great powers will inevitably extend outwards with even less regard, in order to fulfill their desire to slaughter the weak. Not to mention anything else, the situation in the Pacific may stir up huge waves. Although our country can support the past this year, the difficulties in coping with future disasters will be a hundred times greater than today.

Madman

— Ye Lai

When A-Qiang, who was ten years old, returned from the fields carrying a bamboo basket and some weeds, countless frightening shadows surged in his young heart. It was not his biological father's ferocity when he was mad, biting him with teeth that seemed like the mud of the fields, a face that was yellow-black and covered with countless wrinkles. The strange, intense convulsions whenever he jumped up, and the deeply sunken eyes, accustomed to hunger, revealed a terrible, cruel light. The high, hunched shoulders and slightly hunched back were brought back from the mines of Southeast Asia, as if they had long lost his life's vitality. But when he was mad, he would rouse himself and desperately beat his wife and A-Qiang, like a wounded, angry horse, charging blindly at everything that blocked him.

A-Qiang had just returned to the gate of his ancient home. He stepped stealthily, in fact, the little boy's heart was beating terribly, he was afraid of encountering his mad father. But at this moment, his mother was emitting a mournful cry of grief from inside the house. A-Qiang's heart jumped. He didn't dare to run in. His heart knew that this was another of his father's mad tricks. But at this time? The sound of beating and scolding came from the house:

"Damn it, you dare scold me, huh! I'll kill you, what are you? You're a useless stupid pig... huh! I'll kill you! See if you dare scold me..."

His father's roaring voice, followed by the sound of a powerful leg thudding. His mother struggled up and cried out piteously. She moaned in pain:

"Kill me, I don't want to live anymore, I've suffered enough. Heaven! You heartless devil, it's been fourteen years since I came to your house. You went to Southeast Asia for four or five years, and came back like this, mad? You're pretending to be mad! You, you pest, you'll dream of selling all the fields in the family, you don't want to farm, so you let that ghostly woman trick you into going to Southeast Asia. You come back home after four or five years and turn into a mad dog, asking for money every day. Who has the money to support you, you devil, and you're as fierce as a wolf. May Heaven kill you, may lightning strike you, may you die a bad death!"

When A-Qiang timidly ran into the house, he looked in from the corridor into the dark room, a face covered with tears, a haggard and pitiful appearance. Her long hair was pulled apart by his father and was very disheveled. She leaned against the pillar of the old wedding bed as if she had no more life, panting and muttering non-stop. She glared at her husband, who was clenching his teeth, bracing his waist, angrily preparing to hit her again, but when she finished scolding, he laughed grotesquely:

"You shameless ugly woman, you dare to argue? You know, five years ago, my mother died, that's why I sold the land to hold a funeral and pay off some debts. When there was no other way, I did those hateful ×× things, and that's how I met her. She is a woman, a woman with talent, not like you, a stupid pig who doesn't understand anything? Stupid pig! You know, I fled to Southeast Asia to do hard labor for my life. I hid in the mines for more than four years, without earning a single copper coin, and was also whipped by those devils. Ah, look at my back, I'm a hunchback! Look at my shoulders, they're hunched up! This is..." At this point, he suddenly laughed madly, waving his hands, jumping up, clenching his teeth, and roaring: "So, you don't love me anymore? You shameless ugly woman, you're learning from others to have free love! No! You stole a man, you stole a man and that's why you dare scold me like this. You, I went to Southeast Asia for four or five years, and you raised a ten-year-old bastard: A-Qiang, this wild boy, is not yours..."

He gripped his fists madly, jumped in front of her face and roared:

"Get out of here, this is my house, this is my home, go, go, I don't want anything now, just consider that the world has abandoned me. I have no work, Southeast Asia, my hometown, there is no work for me to do, but, I want to drink, I want my freedom, but you don't give me money, are you telling me to die? Didn't you get two or three dimes yesterday from carrying bricks? Where did you take them? Tell me!"

She stood up angrily. She wanted to run away, but he grabbed her with one hand and pushed her and shook her as if he wanted to take a bite. She cried out again, she rushed into his arms and charged wildly, both of them were fighting desperately; but he was stronger, he hugged her neck tightly. He was looking for a kitchen knife while shouting:

"I'm going to use force to chop you to death, chop you to death, you..."

A-Qiang saw this, was startled, and ran out, shouting in terror:

"Help! Dad is going to kill Mom with a knife! Help!..."

After a while, when several neighbors ran into their house, the room was already quiet. He and she were snuggling together, panting, and shedding tears, crying painfully as if they had not been mad...

Page 16

Cattle Market

— Shi Xi

The morning sun climbed to the peak of Cock's Comb Ridge, spitting out a quiet and gentle long tongue, lightly licking the town's towering, thin earth fort. The open space had already begun to fill with people, and the cattle market began. Farmers used trembling, loud voices, shouting at the cattle, passing through the frozen villages, through the barren grasslands, and finally lazily stepping into the town's bleak and dirty main street.

The main street was full of loneliness and cold, and the cattle market was built at the eastern end. The so-called market was a desolate open space, surrounded by some dilapidated fences, on which a few strands of warm sunlight hung tenderly at this time. And under the sunlight, like cow dung, a pile of black crowds was crowded, holding dry tobacco pipes in their hands, talking loudly and indignantly about harvests, market prices, and taxes. The empty and quiet cattle market was filled with smoke, shouts, and roars.

It was ten o'clock. It was the time for the market to open. Uncle Tianfu, the market agent who was also a broker (Note 1), suddenly flew in from somewhere and appeared before the crowd. He was a fat middle-aged man with a "funny spirit," with an odious red nose. As long as his red nose flashed in people's eyes, whoever would recognize him in the midst of thousands of troops and horses: This was Uncle Tianfu's red nose. He stepped over with very generous steps, a gentle smile floating on his face, and a large group of buyers silently followed behind him, touring every corner. He would pat the buttocks of the cattle for his sacred duty, twist their noses, and open their mouths to count their teeth, so they would see the age and value of these cattle.

For the sake of their strategy, the buyers never dared to show satisfaction to the other party. Whenever the agent Uncle Tianfu finished patting a cow's butt or counting its teeth, and said in an inquiring tone, "How about this one?"

They always expressed dissatisfaction, or deliberately shook their heads, but secretly thought, "This is not bad!" But after a while, they would say in an indifferent attitude: "What's the price?"

Uncle Tianfu smiled gently, and beckoned to the cow owner. The cow owner ran over from the crowd, his face glowing with sweat. Uncle Tianfu patted the cow's butt again, and congratulated cheerfully, "Brother Huang Si, this time you're finally going to start the market!"

The one called Huang Si smiled politely and stood straight, but was secretly estimating whether the other party was really sincere in wanting to complete this transaction with him. The other party showed an indifferent attitude, briefly asked him some questions about the cow's life, habits, and labor capacity, and then brought up the price.

The cow owner not only blew a horn for his own cow, for example: "Hey, you see it's a skinny cow, but it has driven fifty fields of millet a day!" Deliberately raising the price a little. The buyer frowned and walked away indifferently, intentionally or unintentionally patting the butt of another cow. At this time, Uncle Tianfu was so frightened that even his red nose turned green, and he followed in a hurry: "How about it?"

The buyer shook his head and shouted angrily, "Damn it! What kind of stuff is this? Worth such a big price!"

"Then you?"

"This!" The buyer stretched out his finger, flicked it lightly in the sun, and walked away.

Uncle Tianfu angrily complained to the cow owner, pointing out that the cow was so old that it could only be dragged into the central stove (Note 2), and after exploring the actual price, ran to find the owner, and after much running and compromise, the goods were finally traded, and Uncle Tianfu took out a red cloth strip from his pocket and tied it to the cow's horn to indicate that it had a new owner, and the cow owner and the buyer smiled and went to the town to drink three cups of wine, which was the customary "transaction" wine. Uncle Tianfu, having received his due amount of compensation, also left to do his other business.

When the sun moved past the middle, the cattle that had not found a new owner were loudly shouted and driven away from the town, passing through the desolate grassland and heading towards the frozen village.

The cattle market's gate was tightly closed, and the town was again filled with desolation and emptiness, only the cold northwest wind roared on the thin earth fort.

Note 1: Broker means public person.

Note 2: Cattle stove is a southern dialect, meaning slaughterhouse.

Movies

Two Blockbusters to Premiere on New Year's Eve in Paris

The Paris Cinema on Avenue Joffre will have a special screening starting at 11:15 PM on New Year's Eve, selected as "Complete Color Cartoon" and "The Count of Monte Cristo" to premiere at the same time. Ticket prices for upstairs and downstairs are two and four corners. The film "The Count of Monte Cristo" was included as a last chance for those who were unable to get tickets due to the crowds these days, as the film is about to be shipped to other cities.

The Grand Cathay Shows "Little Caesar"

James Cagney's latest masterpiece, "Little Caesar" (Frisco Kid), is a tense and exciting martial arts passion epic. Among the recent films starring Cagney, this one is the best, and supporting actors such as Glenda Farrell, Ricardo Cortez, and Lilyan Tashman are all outstanding talents, which adds a lot of color to the film. The film not only has rare and intense battles on the screen, but also the scene of burning down the bandit area, with the fire shining in the sky, which is particularly thrilling. It is now heard that the film has been scheduled to be screened day and night at Guangming today (New Year's Eve). The left is a scene from the film.

Talking about the Ideology of "Triumphant Song"

In the current situation where floods and droughts come one after another, and at a time when we are shouting to eradicate feudal remnants, "Triumphant Song" gives everyone a very alarming hint.

Although it only takes drought as its background, it actually wants to reveal the reasons for the entire so-called "natural disaster" and the real solution. We can see how feudal remnants spread by relying on the manipulation of unscrupulous gentry, and we can also see how the gentry use ignorant peasants to profit from the guise of disaster relief by initiating welcoming god gatherings. Those with a clear mind are regarded as rebels, and good methods cannot be implemented. This makes us know that the mutual use of local tyrants and evil gentry and feudal forces forms a situation where disasters become more serious. The good reputation of disasters is played out in a hypocritical game.

Director Bu Wancang seriously handled this serious subject matter. He used his sophisticated skills to grasp this perfect content and fully developed it, making it deeply imprinted in people's hearts. He used the chaotic crowd scenes to tension the plot, and the climax of finally opening up the river water due to "everyone's unity" is a noteworthy technique.

This film has now been scheduled to be screened at Jincheng on New Year's Day. We introduce it to the ladies of the country with respect and confidence!
